# 🔎┃Overview | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FyY0MAD1pYGO75dm0FhzV%252Flogo%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6ba6fe6-18b1-4894-be5b-55a8ab48982e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9353bb59&sv=2)

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/#the-first-orbital-liquidity-network-and-largest-arbitrum-dex)

The first Orbital Liquidity Network and largest Arbitrum DEX


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Camelot is a decentralized and permissionless exchange that supports the Arbitrum ecosystem with highly efficient liquidity infrastructure. With $30bn volume traded and over 75 partners, Camelot is the leading Arbitrum exchange and a key hub for DeFi activity in the ecosystem. With its foundation firmly set on Arbitrum One, Camelot is expanding its liquidity infrastructure to chains building on the Arbitrum Orbit tech. Through this approach, Camelot creates a cohesive network of aligned rollups and acts as the glue for a diverse and expansive Arbitrum ecosystem.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/#protocol-objectives)

Protocol Objectives

*   Provide the Arbitrum ecosystem with battle-tested and highly efficient spot liquidity infrastructure
    
*   Create a cohesive network of aligned Orbit chains, supporting Arbitrum in becoming the largest hub for Ethereum scaling
    
*   Give users access to the widest range of onchain tokens with deep liquidity, powering highly sustainable yields for liquidity providers
    
*   Onboard and support builders in the Arbitrum ecosystem, with Camelot acting as the central hub for protocols, traders, and the broader community
    
*   Achieve a sustainable economic model that generates value and captures it to the GRAIL token, prioritising real yield
    
*   Build a decentralized and permissionless protocol that puts the community first and is deeply aligned with the Arbitrum ecosystem
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/#initial-foundations)

Initial Foundations

Starting in 2022 and entirely bootstrapped by the Arbitrum community, Camelot has become the largest native DEX by consistently onboarding new users and supporting projects big and small coming to Arbitrum.

Camelot is now the largest protocol exclusive to Arbitrum and has helped over 10 protocols launch, with close relationships to over 65 projects in the ecosystem.

With the expansion of Arbitrum Orbit chains, Camelot has become the first and only protocol to deploy on multiple Orbits. Camelot serves a critical role in providing its battle-tested liquidity infrastructure to these new rollups, now deployed on 8 Orbit chains.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/#becoming-the-orbital-liquidity-network)

Becoming the Orbital Liquidity Network

The Orbital Liquidity Network is Camelot's evolved vision. The Castle will connect and align Orbit chains, creating a unified Arbitrum ecosystem. Most importantly, its role extends beyond just the infrastructure, with Camelot now acting as the hub for these fragmented chains.

Instead of Orbit chains being isolated, Camelot will create network effects so that each chain is connected to the broader Arbitrum community. This will unlock significantly more value for everyone in the network, fueling higher volumes, liquidity, and overall user activity.

Becoming the Orbital Liquidity Network is a significant shift for Camelot and has required months of development to lay the initial foundations. This new vision has brought in a refreshed brand and roadmap to reflect the evolved direction of Camelot.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/#network-vision)

Network Vision

This Orbital Liquidity Network encompasses creating a cohesive and interconnected network of liquidity across multiple Orbit chains, enabling seamless cross-chain transactions, and supporting the broader Arbitrum ecosystem's growth.

Camelot aims to be the central hub where users can easily swap, bridge, and explore various Orbit chains, while continuing to generate sustainable real yields for its token holders.

Through this expansion, Camelot seeks to reduce fragmentation within the ecosystem, align and support builders across different chains, and solidify its role as a key infrastructure provider in the multi-chain future of Arbitrum. Value created by the Orbital Liquidity Network will be captured by GRAIL.

[Next🪐┃Orbital Liquidity Network](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network)

Last updated 10 months ago

# 🪐┃Orbital Liquidity Network | Camelot DEX

Camelot acts as the native decentralized exchange and liquidity hub within the Arbitrum and Orbit Chains ecosystem. It aims to deliver the infrastructure needed for efficient, scalable, and sustainable liquidity across Orbit Chains, playing a vital role in the network's success and expansion

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network#orbit-chains)

Orbit chains

These specialized blockchains leverage Arbitrum’s tech stack. They are designed to offer custom, scalable solutions tailored to specific use cases, such as decentralized finance, gaming, NFTs, and other applications. Chains in this network empower developers with the flexibility to create highly specialized environments, making them ideal for projects that require dedicated ecosystems within the broader Arbitrum network

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network#camelots-mission)

Camelot's mission

Camelot aims to serve as the central hub for Orbit Chains, providing users with a seamless experience to explore and interact with these chains on a single, integrated platform while still maintaining its role as the native Arbitrum DEX. By offering advanced liquidity solutions, Camelot plays a vital role in maintaining the operational efficiency and growth of the network. Its infrastructure is designed not only to meet current demands but also to scale with the network as it expands, ensuring effective liquidity management across the entire ecosystem

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network#vision)

Vision

As Orbit Chains continue to evolve, Camelot will remain a cornerstone of the network’s growth. By providing efficient and scalable liquidity solutions, Camelot ensures that Orbit Chains can continue to innovate and expand. This positions Camelot as an essential component of the ecosystem and a key driver of future developments within the Orbit network, with its strategic importance only increasing as the network scales

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network#upcoming-orbital-network-related-integrations)

Upcoming Orbital network-related integrations

*   **Cross-Chain Swaps**
    
    A seamless cross-chain swap system integrated into the app, enabling users to trade assets between Orbit chains effortlessly. This feature ensures smooth interoperability across multiple chains within the Orbit network, reinforcing Camelot as the ultimate Orbital liquidity hub
    
*   **Gauges** A system allowing xGRAIL holders to vote on the allocation of incentives to liquidity pools across Arbitrum and Orbit Chains
    
*   **Accelerator** The Accelerator xGRAIL Plugin will act as an incubator for new projects within the Arbitrum and Orbit ecosystems. Unlike a traditional launchpad, this plugin will focus on accelerating the growth, providing them with the necessary tools and support to thrive in the Arbitrum and Orbit ecosystems
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network#explore-orbit-chains-connected-to-camelot)

Explore Orbit Chains connected to Camelot

# Corn | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FRFgNazhLJx3UWljRbCRI%252F4836a89d-ce8e-4572-97b1-8cfcd188f604.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fbf6246-ad44-4477-9128-01a1eceea893&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e74d9ae1&sv=2)

[Website](https://usecorn.com/)

[Chain Explorer](https://cornscan.io/)

[X](https://x.com/use_corn)

[Discord](https://discord.com/invite/usecorn)

[Telegram](https://t.me/+upkPwAJwIz5iZDEx)

[Corn is](https://blog.usecorn.com/introducing-corn-the-super-yield-network-built-around-digital-gold-01436745b64a)
 an Ethereum Layer 2 network powered by Arbitrum Orbit, designed to bring Bitcoin into the heart of DeFi. It uses tokenized Bitcoin (BTCN) as its gas token, seamlessly bridging Bitcoin and Ethereum ecosystems. BTCN, pegged 1:1 with Bitcoin, offers flexible custody options, while the governance token CORN empowers stakers to influence network rewards

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/corn#connect-your-wallet-to-corn)

Connect your wallet to Corn


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

Corn

RPC URL

[https://rpc.ankr.com/corn\_maizenet](https://rpc.ankr.com/corn_maizenet)

Chain ID

21000000

Currency symbol

BTCN

Block explorer URL

[https://cornscan.io](https://cornscan.io/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Corn chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/corn#bridge-to-corn)

Bridge to Corn

Tokens can be bridged to the Corn chain using the official [bridge](https://usecorn.com/app?action=bridge)

Gas on the Corn chain is paid in BTCN Therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

[Get BTCN](https://docs.usecorn.com/docs/users/User_Guides/Get_BTCN/)

[How to bridge](https://docs.usecorn.com/docs/users/User_Guides/Bridge/)
 ℹ️

[PreviousApeChain](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/apechain)
[NextDegen](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/degen)

Last updated 10 months ago

# ApeChain | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJN20E5PB8QtBPdMxlSee%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D454ed918-8b77-4d18-8baf-765ab08e859a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebfb84f2&sv=2)

[Website](https://apechain.com/)

[Chain Explorer](https://apechain.calderaexplorer.xyz/)

[X](https://x.com/apecoin)

[Discord](https://discord.gg/apecoindao)

[Telegram](https://t.me/apechainofficial)

ApeChain is a next-generation Layer 3 blockchain, meticulously crafted by ApeLabs to redefine the gaming and digital collectibles landscape. Powered by Arbitrum Orbit technology, ApeChain offers unparalleled performance with lightning-fast transaction speeds, low latency, and robust security, making it the perfect foundation for cutting-edge gaming applications and thriving NFT ecosystems. Engineered for flexibility, the chain supports both permissioned and permissionless environments, fostering a vibrant space where innovation can flourish

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/apechain#connect-your-wallet-to-apechain)

Connect your wallet to ApeChain


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

ApeChain

RPC URL

[https://apechain.calderachain.xyz/http](https://apechain.calderachain.xyz/http)

Chain ID

33139

Currency symbol

APE

Block explorer URL

[https://apechain.calderaexplorer.xyz/](https://apechain.calderaexplorer.xyz/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the ApeChain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/apechain#bridge-to-apechain)

Bridge to ApeChain

Tokens can be bridged to ApeChain using the official Ape bridge or [multi-chain Stargate](https://stargate.finance/bridge)

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for bridging fees from any supported chain to ApeChain

Gas on the ApeChain is paid in APE. Therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

1.  Visit the [Ape bridge](https://apechain.com/portal#bridge)
     and connect your wallet. You will see the screen below:
    
    ![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fnhh0sySDewiDYzJaE6Jl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc07fa710-2a8b-4a74-a39f-15f573f5fce1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=22d238ab&sv=2)
    

2\. Select the token/network and input the amount you want to transfer to ApeChain and click Bridge

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FteGD7H7YmNcxvpttvQYZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db89ed16c-7a0b-4016-9933-aaf1b80881ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b9d57e4&sv=2)

1.  Approve, then proceed with the transfer, which will require confirmation in your wallet interface
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FbC5xS02oOJ2TwcCKrXab%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D157bde16-c923-4945-9d34-e75a7b142187&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=101175b0&sv=2)

1.  After the transfer is complete, you will see a confirmation like the one shown below
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FrYKQf8oPI8JpweqSsJY9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D053df93d-0ca7-4e9d-884b-08221ea24172&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6890eeec&sv=2)

The bridging transfer should take approximately 3 minutes, but it may take longer during periods of high traffic

# Degen | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FkneIXlGMAW29WDVB8BX4%252FUntitled%2520design%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71bcc519-f269-4310-af2a-299352b920af&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac76bfa3&sv=2)

[X](https://x.com/degentokenbase)

[Telegram](https://t.me/degentokenbase)

Degen Chain is a Layer 3 blockchain powered by Arbitrum Orbit, designed to empower the Degen community with ultra-low transaction fees and lightning-fast performance. It seamlessly integrates with Base, an Ethereum Layer 2, for secure and efficient transaction settlements. The chain’s native token $DEGEN, fuels its ecosystem, enabling activities like token swaps, staking, and farming

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/degen#connect-your-wallet-to-the-degen-chain)

Connect your wallet to the Degen chain


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

Degen

RPC URL

[https://rpc.degen.tips](https://rpc.degen.tips/)

Chain ID

666666666

Currency symbol

DEGEN

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.degen.tips/](https://explorer.degen.tips/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Degen chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/degen#bridge-to-degen)

Bridge to Degen

Tokens can be bridged to the Degen chain using the

Gas on the Degen chain is paid in DEGEN Therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

Tokens can be bridged using the official [Degen bridge](https://bridge.degen.tips/)
 or [multi-chain Stargate](https://stargate.finance/bridge?srcChain=arbitrum&srcToken=0x9F07F8A82cB1af1466252e505b7b7ddee103bC91&dstChain=degen&dstToken=0xEeeeeEeeeEeEeeEeEeEeeEEEeeeeEeeeeeeeEEeE)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FrIGle4WeDcIq6f2JQlPq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D842dc246-c958-4271-b5ba-1ae887a5ece7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96c4c550&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FwLq9UBvu2jHUbFKjKGYI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D810674af-e794-4341-a0e2-e77e9f342d42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=669f952d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F3Q83fWSoOTK1XYdXbqwe%252FUntitled%2520design%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d116dfb-faa7-4273-854f-b4a3fd887e79&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13d7fb2a&sv=2)

[Website](https://duckchain.io/)

[Chain Explorer](https://scan.duckchain.io/)

[X](https://x.com/Duck_Chain)

[Telegram](https://t.me/DuckChainAnn)

DuckChain is an advanced Layer 3 blockchain crafted to enhance DeFi and gaming within the TON ecosystem. Powered by Arbitrum Orbit technology, it delivers fast, cost-efficient, and secure transactions. Fully compatible with Ethereum's Virtual Machine (EVM), DuckChain bridges TON and Ethereum, enabling seamless interoperability and improved liquidity. Its flexible design supports both permissioned and open environments, making it a practical solution for a variety of applications

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/duckchain#connect-your-wallet-to-duckchain)

Connect your wallet to DuckChain


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

DuckChain

RPC URL

[https://rpc.duckchain.io](https://rpc.duckchain.io/)

Chain ID

5545

Currency symbol

TON

Block explorer URL

[https://scan.duckchain.io/](https://scan.duckchain.io/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the DuckChain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/duckchain#bridge-to-duckchain)

Bridge to DuckChain

Tokens can be bridged to the DuckChain using the official [Duck bridge](https://bridge.duckchain.io/)
 or multi-chain [Meson bridge](https://meson.fi/)

Gas on the DuckChain is paid in TON Therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

1.  Visit the [Duck bridge](https://bridge.duckchain.io/)
     and connect your wallet You will see the screen below:
    
    ![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F6H8ZkGyOGChv5qdTwWQy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ce5e122-1948-4bff-abf3-f386be41dbc4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1961bbd4&sv=2)
    
2.  Select the token/network and input the amount you want to transfer and click Deposit
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FT5OaURrcPvmHoVRNZlNM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38835eed-aeae-4a5b-9a90-2f9d60c2c16f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=574a6ae&sv=2)

1.  Input recipient DuckChain address or connect wallet and click Deposit
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJcaa95FU9MiO9g5vN5Pv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da996d0df-7633-4885-b933-8cc793d77869&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ccf90c2&sv=2)

1.  Ensure that the recipient address is correct and confirm deposit
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F4JSOUuVYhH6BmvhPHxNT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea381f05-8ca2-44ee-a3fb-fe845d8cd153&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6093fac1&sv=2)

1.  After the deposit is succesfull, you will see a confirmation like the one shown below
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F12uhwhCGIcYl0iSi0BJg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8c3f488-3f5c-44d7-b4e2-0b33783d38c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb73bc0&sv=2)

The bridging transfer should take approximately 5 - 20 minutes, but it may take longer during periods of high traffic

# 📅┃Launch & Genesis | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FRWwPv8LfZhLds1ER86LQ%252FCamelot%2520Roadmap.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5872b57-a737-40c6-9060-4e8b49508fe4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b6e66be&sv=2)

Camelot was designed to be community-driven, and the GRAIL token's launch sequence was a significant factor in achieving that goal. The team remained committed to building the best product possible before seeking funding. The public sale provided a transparent and fair opportunity for the community, investors, and partners to purchase GRAIL

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/launch-and-genesis#fair-launch)

Fair launch


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The public sale began on November 29th **2022** and ended on December 5th, with GRAIL liquidity going live 24 hours after the sale ended

*   The auction mechanism started with a fully diluted valuation (FDV) of $2m, fixing a $20 floor price for GRAIL, and increased after the first $300k was raised
    
*   The public sale offered 15% of the GRAIL supply (15,000 out of 100,000 tokens in total), with 10% in GRAIL and 5% in xGRAIL
    
*   There was no pre-sale or VC investment
    
*   All purchases were settled at the same price based on the total amount deposited
    
*   There was no hard cap on the public sale and no limit on how much USDC could be allocated per wallet
    
*   Users could share a referral link and claim 3% of all referred investments made through it after the launch - Refferal commissions were funded from allocated supply to [Core Contributors](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/token-distribution)
    
*   Legacy token holders ([lEXC](https://camelotdex.medium.com/onboarding-v1-holders-to-camelot-on-arbitrum-74305c6c1a45)
    ) were eligible for a 10% discount during the public sale
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/launch-and-genesis#the-public-sale-results)

[**The public sale results**](https://app.camelot.exchange/launchpad/camelot)

*   Total raised: $3,796,460.86
    
*   GRAIL price: $254.21
    
*   Circulating market cap: $5,719,727.37
    
*   Fully diluted valuation (FDV): $25,421,010.52
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FGWpEtqjYvlPNPtUYorOr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cedfe7a-cec3-4ebc-adff-03ba6958d8c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=316e814b&sv=2)

**The public sale proceeds were directed as follows:**

*   50% was paired with 7.5% of GRAIL from POL in UNI v2-style liquidity
    
*   30% allocated to xGRAIL real yield staking treasury
    
*   20% was used to support the Camelot team, which had been entirely self-funded up till the launch
    

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/launch-and-genesis#genesis-pools)

Genesis pools


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Genesis pools were created to serve as exclusive farms for early adopters. The purpose of these farms was to bootstrap initial liquidity for Camelot before GRAIL went live while providing an early and attractive opportunity for the community to accumulate xGRAIL

*   Genesis pools were open for deposits from November 22nd, and rewards started being allocated to depositors from November 23rd
    
*   Depositors were earning emissions in xGRAIL linearly during the six months following the public sale and could withdraw anytime, with their share of the emissions redirected to the remaining participants
    
*   In some cases, genesis farm distributed not only xGRAIL but also incentives from a second token, usually provided by a partner protocol
    
*   The Genesis farms are based on the existing Nitro pool reward structure
    

Genesis Pools emissions ceased on the 23rd of May 2023

[PreviousXAI](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/xai)
[Next📞┃Contact us](https://docs.camelot.exchange/contact-us)

Last updated 1 year ago

[https://molten.bridge.caldera.xyz/](https://molten.bridge.caldera.xyz/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Molten chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/molten#bridge-to-molten)

Bridge to Molten

Tokens can be bridged to Molten using Caldera bridge

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for bridging fees from Arbitrum to Molten

Gas on the Molten chain is paid in MOLTEN - therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

1.  Visit the [Caldera bridge](https://molten.bridge.caldera.xyz/)
     and connect your wallet. Ensure your wallet is set up for Arbitrum. You will see the screen below:
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FPerdVu8Z0FjtLoGQFXdT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a47a3a2-33d9-4e9c-b984-7e49c4df2c0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3996bff4&sv=2)

1.  Input the amount of MOLTEN (or any other token) you want to transfer to Molten chain and click Transfer Tokens
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FVHMZQfWG5aKGVaOkhyKw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4846a39-2da6-4635-a8e3-aa792164726b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bafa147a&sv=2)

1.  Approve, then initiate the transfer, which will require confirmation in your wallet interface
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FmGgUKnKoAqQq1zCk4ja1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00591f5b-2f2e-4653-a4d9-ab1c325b7bfd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=339d9e71&sv=2)

1.  The transaction will show as pending on the Transactions page
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fi6DWIvdV4FKonJN54EVK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De109abe5-84af-4af7-ac28-35434707de62&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=210bf09b&sv=2)

The bridging transfer should take approximately 15 minutes, but it may take longer during periods of high traffic

# Superposition | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FvqbfRBklP4ls3nFtku0Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb95968a-42e0-408b-ae35-0f96edc1a43b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=815d7fd9&sv=2)

[X](https://x.com/Superpositionso)

Superposition Chain is a pioneering DeFi-native Layer 3 blockchain designed to reward both users and developers for their participation. Built on Arbitrum Orbit, it introduces innovative incentive mechanisms such as Utility Mining and Super Assets, which generate yield through both holding and active usage. The platform features a native on-chain order book, leveraging Stylus for faster execution speeds, and provides shared, permissionless liquidity across all decentralized applications within its ecosystem

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/superposition#connect-your-wallet-to-superposition)

Network name

Superposition

RPC URL

Chain ID

55244

Currency symbol

ETH

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.superposition.so/](https://explorer.superposition.so/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Superposition chain

# Reya | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FyMhEnmAujTPeXVSLUExg%252FReya%2520Banner.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6840535-19ae-4d47-8c0f-44f9bc9ce826&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4e9179&sv=2)

[Website](https://reya.network/)

[Chain Explorer](https://explorer.reya.network/)

[Discord](https://discord.gg/reyaxyz)

[X](https://x.com/reya_xyz)

The Reya Network, developed by Reya Labs and supported by a team of DeFi pioneers, was purpose-built to address the unique challenges of DeFi trading at scale. Optimized specifically for trading, this Layer 2 blockchain enhances liquidity through a novel passive liquidity pool mechanism, enabling shared liquidity across all exchanges in its ecosystem. Reya Network also offers advanced capital efficiency by embedding margin engine logic directly into the network, allowing users to manage a single margin account across multiple exchanges. With its lightning-fast transaction speeds, zero gas fees, and a first-in-first-out (FIFO) execution model, Reya Network provides a seamless and high-performance trading experience

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/reya#connect-your-wallet-to-reya)

Connect your wallet to Reya


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

Reya

RPC URL

[https://rpc.reya.network](https://rpc.reya.network/)

Chain ID

1729

Currency symbol

ETH

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.reya.network](https://explorer.reya.network/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Reya chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/reya#bridge-to-reya)

Bridge to Reya

Tokens can be bridged to Reya using the official Reya bridge.

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for bridging fees from any supported chain to Reya

wETH from Socket is used as the main asset in the liquidity pools

Gas on the Reya chain is paid in ETH - therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

1.  Visit the [Reya Bridge](https://reya.network/bridge)
     and connect your wallet. You will see the screen below:
    
    ![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FvoxrGD6t4e8IbbhlkhNP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac52b87f-5b6a-4bf5-a09d-52509ad5c072&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e8c2bf3&sv=2)
    

2\. Input the amount of w/ETH (or any other token) you want to transfer to Reya, trigger the Approve token and then Bridge

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fco8FUOLMD00F8H0VhIJh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74a77feb-a345-4764-9bfe-7c503f209ff7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91497737&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FYoxAMSDQa1dnWpPb2d8G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc00c9f2e-97b6-4b83-9f8c-45f108ee026a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8d8ee56&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJsJvxIQCtDzTA4NpRwuk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f85b8de-4a6f-4bc5-b944-e55cf77f36ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8718cd1&sv=2)

4\. The transaction will appear as pending in the top right corner of the page

The bridging transfer should take approximately 15 minutes, but it may take longer during periods of high traffic

[PreviousRari](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/rari)
[NextSanko](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/sanko)

# Sanko | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Ff2Gy25stC8ebpZOFhi1I%252FSanko%2520Banner.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69e02afa-12a7-4a52-9149-d11d9432e7ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73ab7d73&sv=2)

[Website](https://sanko.xyz/)

[Chain Explorer](https://explorer.sanko.xyz/)
 / [B](https://tools.sanko.xyz/)

[Discord](https://discord.gg/Cnz62Vfa2C)

[Telegram](https://t.me/sankogamecorp)

[X](https://x.com/SankoGameCorp)

The Sanko Chain is purposefully designed to meet the demands of gaming economies at scale. As a Layer 3 blockchain, it enables seamless integration with interoperable in-game experiences, offering players and developers a tailored environment that supports high transaction throughput with minimal fees. Sanko abstracts the complexities of blockchain, providing gamers with an enhanced user experience while giving developers access to increased gas and contract capabilities

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/sanko#connect-your-wallet-to-sanko)

Connect your wallet to Sanko


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

Sanko

RPC URL

[https://sanko-mainnet.calderachain.xyz/http](https://sanko-mainnet.calderachain.xyz/http)

Chain ID

1996

Currency symbol

DMT

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.sanko.xyz/](https://explorer.sanko.xyz/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Sanko chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/sanko#bridge-to-sanko)

Bridge to Sanko

Tokens can be bridged to Sanko using Sanko bridge

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for bridging fees from Arbitrum to Sanko

Gas on the Sanko chain is paid in DMT - therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

Any ERC-20 tokens compatible with Arbitrum can be bridged to Sanko - you must input and add the contract address of the token before initiating the bridging process

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FGIcUsvebfzrjWLmxIHWK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b0fd26f-4b6c-4ab7-9516-be839e198fe1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5ac109dd&sv=2)

1.  Visit the [Sanko Bridge](https://sanko.xyz/bridge)
     and connect your wallet. Ensure your wallet is set up for Arbitrum. You will see the screen below:
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FZUhb6ZhH4IacASRU2bAx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df653a528-576b-4951-bed7-231a2a90f327&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bbc751e&sv=2)

1.  Input the amount of DMT (or any other token) you want to transfer to Sanko chain and click Move funds to Sanko
    
2.  Approve and Bridge
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F204YAUNMXBR1sexM8vFy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8de14923-9522-4ddc-8010-a1a6d9b5d12b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a93f3551&sv=2)

4\. Confirm the transaction in your wallet

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FmGgUKnKoAqQq1zCk4ja1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00591f5b-2f2e-4653-a4d9-ab1c325b7bfd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=339d9e71&sv=2)

5\. The transaction will show as pending on the next page

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FYm1iKcmXiZYifrFZH9Wk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc30ff0fc-7af1-429a-a730-6e22c79f33e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b05a2a9&sv=2)

Bear in mind the relevant waiting periods for deposits (5min) and withdrawals (up to 7 days)

Deposits to Sanko are automatically sent to the wallet, while withdrawals need to be claimed in the pending transactions section of the bridge app

# Gravity | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FSIR7CO3eCG701FuvYMw7%252FUntitled%2520design%2520%2838%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28be38e3-6010-4c76-adbc-6260aee27494&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a7436626&sv=2)

[Website](https://gravity.xyz/)

[Chain Explorer](https://www.okx.com/web3/explorer/gravity-alpha)

[Discord](https://discord.gg/GravityChain)

[Telegram](http://t.me/GravityChain)

[X](https://x.com/GravityChain)

The Gravity Chain, developed by Galxe, is a Layer 1 blockchain engineered to revolutionize cross-chain interactions at scale. Specifically designed for mass adoption, this blockchain abstracts the complexities of multi-chain transactions, providing a seamless and secure experience for both developers and users. Gravity integrates cutting-edge technologies like Zero-Knowledge Proofs and the Jolteon consensus algorithm, ensuring high throughput, near-instant finality, and robust security

By offering advanced features such as gas abstraction and full EVM compatibility, Gravity empowers developers to deploy smart contracts effortlessly while enhancing the overall user experience. Integrated deeply within the Galxe ecosystem, Gravity serves as the backbone for a wide array of decentralized applications, making it a pivotal force in the evolution of Web3

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/gravity#connect-your-wallet-to-gravity)

Connect your wallet to Gravity


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

Gravity

RPC URL

[https://rpc.gravity.xyz](https://rpc.gravity.xyz/)

Chain ID

1625

Currency symbol

G

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.gravity.xyz](https://explorer.gravity.xyz/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the Gravity chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/gravity#bridge-to-gravity)

Bridge to Gravity

Tokens can be bridged to Gravity using the official Gravity bridge or [multi-chain Stargate bridge](https://stargate.finance/bridge)

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for bridging fees from any supported chain to Gravity

Gas on the Gravity chain is paid in G, which can currently only be obtained on the Ethereum chain. Therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

To bridge USDC, USDT, or wETH, use the [Stargate bridge](https://stargate.finance/bridge)
. For G, use the bridge below

     and connect your wallet. You will see the screen below:

# XAI | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F0EiccqnCUmhfc7cxTdHG%252FXAI%2520banner.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b1cb8b4-4a84-4d03-b616-49aa673ec889&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=856888de&sv=2)

[Website](https://xai.games/)

[Chain Explorer](https://explorer.xai-chain.net/)
 / [B](https://www.ondora.xyz/network/xai/interactions)

[Discord](https://discord.com/invite/xaigames)

[Telegram](https://t.me/XaiSentryNodes)

[X](https://twitter.com/XAI_GAMES)

The Xai Blockchain, developed by Offchain Labs and overseen by the Xai Foundation, was custom-developed to address the needs of web3 gaming at scale. Tailored specifically for gaming, this blockchain offers traditional gamers an abstracted wallet and account experience, provides developers with increased gas and contract limits, and establishes a fully decentralized ecosystem that fosters trust and transparency for all participants. By leveraging Ethereum's robust security measures, the XAI chain cements its resilience against potential hacks and other vulnerabilities

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/xai#connect-your-wallet-to-xai)

Connect your wallet to XAI


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

Xai Mainnet

RPC URL

[https://xai-chain.net/rpc](https://xai-chain.net/rpc)

Chain ID

660279

Currency symbol

XAI

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.xai-chain.net/](https://explorer.xai-chain.net/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the XAI chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/xai#bridge-to-xai)

Bridge to XAI

Tokens can be bridged to XAI using the official Arbitrum bridge.

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for bridging fees from Arbitrum to XAI

Gas on the Xai chain is paid in XAI - therefore, we recommend bridging it as the first token so you can process transactions

Any ERC-20 tokens compatible with Arbitrum can be bridged to XAI - you must input and add the contract address of the token before initiating the bridging process

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FxP30TjprAaWyLmGArbcX%252F01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a2260b5-9450-4903-ba69-0fee35931b45&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8964ba32&sv=2)

     and connect your wallet. Ensure your wallet is set up for Arbitrum. You will see the screen below:
    
    ![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FF1W1WFv2UbJq79CiKdUa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcbc51e2f-4f02-48ec-a3d2-d0fe0627598a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2de2b611&sv=2)

# Security Measures | Camelot DEX

Camelot's expertly crafted smart contracts are developed by seasoned professionals with a deep understanding of the industry. We prioritize the safety and optimization of your investments by incorporating a robust set of features and security measures. Camelot's comprehensive range of features has been thoroughly audited by one of the most reputable firms in the business - Paladin. As the leading smart contract security firm, Paladin provides the most sophisticated and all-encompassing auditing services available in the industry.

To review the detailed info on the audit, please follow this [link](https://docs.camelot.exchange/references/audits)

To further bolster the security of the protocol, Camelot has implemented multisig, short for multi-signature, which is a type of digital signature that combines multiple unique signatures. This ensures that funds stored on a multi-signature address can only be accessed when two or more signatures are provided simultaneously. The use of multisig wallets provides an additional layer of security, and by utilizing multisig, we can avoid the problems often associated with single-key wallets.

For a comprehensive overview of multisig addresses, please visit the following [page](https://docs.camelot.exchange/references/multisigs)

# V2 Stable Pools Explained | Camelot DEX

Pools holding assets at the same price are called stable pools. Camelot **V2** stable pools are based on solidly maths. A [dual-liquidity](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm/dual-liquidity-type)
 model is built directly into the Camelot core, which supports both stable pools with assets that are correlated with each other as well as volatile pools with uncorrelated assets.

Stable pools concentrate most of their liquidity at current prices, so they use it more efficiently. As trades occur, the pool can adjust the price so as to move the highest liquidity region without incurring losses.

The stable swaps tend to stick to the 1:1 ratio as much as possible until a certain point where they revert to a xyk curve when impossible. To move away from a 1:1 swap ratio, the liquidity ratio spread must be way more pronounced compared to a xyk curve

The process of becoming a liquidity provider in a stable pool is the same as that in a volatile pool. As a liquidity provider in a stable pool, you will gain exposure to all assets in the pool and will incur risk as well.

Calculations are used to maintain the liquidity of the pool at all times using mathematical formulas

*   x is the amount of the first asset in the pool
    
*   y is the amount of the second asset in the pool
    
*   k is a fixed value
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FDa42phLttmChtUBXEfKY%252Fstable%2520pools%2520formulas.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37300391-3058-4faf-ab70-fd22408e526e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e13e725&sv=2)

An illustration of how the stable purple and volatile orange AMM pricing calculations compare is presented below. It shows:

# GRAIL and xGRAIL plugins | Camelot DEX

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#how-can-i-obtain-grail)

**How can I obtain** [**GRAIL**](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/grail-token)
**?**

GRAIL can be purchased through the [exchange](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-explained)
 tab or earned through farming

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#what-is-the-process-for-obtaining-xgrail)

**What is the process for obtaining** [**xGRAIL**](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token)
**?**

GRAIL can be [converted](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/get-xgrail)
 to xGRAIL at a 1:1 ratio under the xGRAIL tab. Additionally, xGRAIL can be earned from incentivized farms

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#what-is-the-value-of-xgrail)

**What is the value of xGRAIL?**

GRAIL is illiquid, and its value is directly correlated to the GRAIL value. One xGRAIL equals one GRAIL

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#does-grail-have-a-capped-supply)

**Does GRAIL have a capped supply?**

Yes, GRAIL will reach its hard cap somewhere around 2027. [Deflationary mechanisms](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/deflationary-mechanisms)
 have also been implemented to reduce the total supply

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#does-xgrail-have-a-capped-supply)

**Does xGRAIL have a capped supply?**

xGRAIL is an essentially wrapped GRAIL and does not have its own maximum supply. The number of xGRAILs in circulation is equal to the number of GRAIL

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#can-i-swap-xgrail-for-any-other-token)

**Can I swap xGRAIL for any other token?**

xGRAIL is not transferable. You can only redeem it to GRAIL

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#how-long-does-it-take-for-xgrail-to-redeem-vest)

**How long does it take for xGRAIL to redeem (vest)?**

[The minimum vesting duration is 15 days (50% GRAIL output), and the maximum duration is 180 days (100% GRAIL output). As your xGRAIL vests, 50% of the amount is automatically staked in real yield staking plugin, earning you rewards during the vesting period](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/redeem-xgrail)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#xgrail-plugins)

xGRAIL plugins

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#how-can-i-utilize-the-xgrail-tab)

**How can I utilize the xGRAIL tab?**

*   Convert GRAIL to xGRAIL
    
*   Redeem xGRAIL to GRAIL through vesting
    
*   Allocate xGRAIL to real yield staking plugin to earn rewards
    
*   Allocate xGRAIL through yield booster to boost your positions APR
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#what-are-the-benefits-of-yield-booster-and-how-does-it-work)

**What are the benefits of yield booster, and how does it work?**

The yield booster allows boosting emissions APR by allocating xGRAIL to an LP. The boost in xGRAIL allocation depends on the number of users allocating to a particular asset

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#how-are-real-yield-staking-rewards-distributed)

**How are** real yield staking rewards **distributed?**

A portion of the transaction fees is distributed as xgrail staking rewards every week. Rewards are distributed continuously meaning that you can harvest pending rewards at any point

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/grail-and-xgrail-plugins#does-the-real-yield-staking-epoch-cycle-always-consist-of-7-days)

**Does the** real yield staking **epoch (cycle) always consist of 7 days?**

Yes, the epoch always lasts for 7 days

# Understanding Impermanent Loss | Camelot DEX

At its core, impermanent loss is the difference in potential earnings between holding tokens in an AMM and simply holding them in your wallet. Impermanent loss occurs when the price of tokens inside a pool deviates from when they were initially deposited. If the prices return to their initial state, the loss is impermanent since the value returns to its original state. Although, if the prices remain diverged, the loss becomes permanent.

Though such losses can be offset by trading fees earned from liquidity provision, a clear understanding of impermanent loss dynamics remains crucial.

For a comprehensive understanding of IL, consider reading this detailed [article](https://cointelegraph.com/explained/what-is-impermanent-loss-and-how-to-avoid-it)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/understanding-impermanent-loss#how-to-avoid-impermanent-loss)

**How to avoid Impermanent Loss?**

*   Impermanent loss occurs when there is a significant price difference between the assets in the liquidity pool. Therefore, you should consider the historical price movement and volatility of the assets before providing liquidity. If the assets are known to have high volatility or price fluctuations, you may want to choose a wider price range to reduce the risk of impermanent loss (Applies only to V3)
    
*   Use correlation analysis to determine the relationship between the assets you're providing liquidity for: _\- If the assets are highly correlated, it may reduce the risk of impermanent loss - If the assets have a low correlation, it may increase the risk of impermanent loss_
    
*   Liquidity pool size and trading volume can affect the risk of impermanent loss. Generally, larger liquidity pools and higher trading volumes can reduce the risk of impermanent loss. You can use [analytics](https://info.camelot.exchange/pairs/v3)
     page to analyze historical trading volumes and liquidity pool size to determine the best liquidity pools to provide liquidity for
    
*   Impermanent loss is an ongoing risk, and you should monitor your liquidity pools regularly to adjust your strategy as necessary. This may involve rebalancing your liquidity, adjusting your price ranges, or withdrawing liquidity altogether
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/understanding-impermanent-loss#understanding-impermanent-loss-in-v3)

Understanding Impermanent Loss in V3

*   Because the concentrated liquidity model allows LPs to provide liquidity at specific price points, they may be exposed to more risk from price volatility than in V2
    
*   If the price of the assets being provided liquidity for moves outside of the price range where liquidity is concentrated, LPs may face more significant losses
    
*   An impermanent loss is realized if the deposited assets change in price since the deposit
    
*   There is no impermanent loss if the price returns to its initial level
    
*   If you remove your funds from the liquidity pool before the price returns to its original level, the impermanent loss will become permanent
    

**Example A: Narrow range**

*   Lancelot provides liquidity for a token pair (ETH and USDC) with a range of $1000-$1500
    
*   As long as the price stays within $1000-$1500, Lancelot earns fees from trades
    
*   If the price of the assets being provided liquidity for moves outside of the price range where liquidity is concentrated, Lancelot's LP may face more significant losses
    

**Example B: Wide range**

*   Robin provides liquidity for the same token pair with a range of $500-$2500
    
*   Robin's range is larger, so he earns fees from a wider price movement, but his money works less efficiently
    
*   If the price stays within $500-$2500, Robin will have a smaller chance of experiencing impermanent loss compared to Lancelot's small range
    

**Example C: Out of Range** _(Manual mode)_

*   Galahad provides liquidity for the token pair with a range of $800-$1200 (ETH-USDC)
    
*   If the price goes up to $1200, Galahad will hold only USDC
    
*   If the price later drops to $1000, Galahad would have an impermanent loss because he had less exposure to ETH when the price was within his range
    

In simpler terms, impermanent loss when providing liquidity to V3 depends on the price range you choose and how the asset's price changes. By picking a wider range, you can reduce the chance of impermanent loss, but you may also earn less from trading fees

**Example D:** _(Auto mode - Gamma)_

*   [_Gamma document_](https://docs.gamma.xyz/gamma/features/strategies#impermanent-loss)
    [_ation_](https://docs.gamma.xyz/gamma/features/strategies#impermanent-loss)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/understanding-impermanent-loss#does-the-single-sided-liquidity-provision-in-v3-eliminate-the-risk-of-impermanent-loss)

Does the single-sided liquidity provision in V3 eliminate the risk of impermanent loss?

While it does help reduce the impact of impermanent loss, it doesn't completely eliminate the possibility of risk. Providing liquidity still carries certain risks, including price volatility and fluctuations in the market

# 📘┃Arbitrum Guide | Camelot DEX

Arbitrum is built by [Offchain Labs](https://offchainlabs.com/)
, which consists of world-class blockchain engineers, researchers, and Ethereum experts. Arbitrum One main net launched on the 31st of August 2021.

*   Arbitrum serves as Ethereum's next-generation layer-2.
    
*   The layer-2 solution facilitates transactions through off-chain means before bundling and submitting them as a single transaction to the base layer, thus supporting Ethereum scaling. As a result, layer-1 Ethereum transactions will not be slowed down by many transaction requests.
    
*   Arbitrum is an Optimistic Rollup solution. Optimistic rollups are smart contracts that bundle transactions, reducing computation time and gas consumption. By utilizing Optimistic Rollups, Arbitrum can ensure inexpensive gas fees while relying on Ethereum's L1 security.
    
*   Arbitrum successfully migrated the existing Arbitrum One network to Arbitrum Nitro on the 31st of August, 2022.
    
*   On March 23, Arbitrum distributed its highly-anticipated $ARB governance token.
    

As with any other chain, Arbitrum has a similar onboarding process. Adding support for Arbitrum to your wallet is all you need to do, and then you can transfer funds to the network through one of the bridges that offer Arbitrum transfer support or send funds from a centralized exchange.

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide#be-aware-that-all-transaction-fees-on-arbitrum-are-payable-in-eth)

Be aware that all transaction fees on Arbitrum are payable in ETH

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide#now-that-weve-covered-arbitrum-lets-learn-about)

Now that we've covered Arbitrum let's learn about

[Wallet Creation](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/wallet-creation)
[Wallet Setup for Arbitrum Compatibility](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/wallet-setup-for-arbitrum-compatibility)
[Bridging tokens to Arbitrum](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/bridging-tokens-to-arbitrum)
[Adding tokens to the wallet interface](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/adding-tokens-to-the-wallet-interface)

[PreviousSecurity Measures](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/security-measures)
[NextWallet Creation](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/wallet-creation)

# Proof of play Apex | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F8r2JtuYOUuHXFobfSAO5%252FUntitled%2520design%2520%2835%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b79600a-249a-47ea-8961-cea6b03d2a30&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76be3164&sv=2)

[Website](https://www.proofofplay.com/)

[Chain Explorer](https://explorer.apex.proofofplay.com/)

[Discord](https://discord.com/invite/piratenation)

[X](https://twitter.com/ProofOfPlay/)

The Apex Chain, developed by Proof of Play, is a Layer 2 blockchain engineered to meet the demands of decentralized gaming at scale. Utilizing Arbitrum Orbit tech stack, this blockchain offers a frictionless, gasless, and signless experience, making blockchain gaming accessible and seamless for players. Developers benefit from high transaction throughput and the chain's unique mirroring technology, which allows for secure Layer 1 trading while gameplay occurs on Layer 2

Apex Chain is the backbone of games like Pirate Nation, where players truly own and control their in-game assets, all stored permanently on-chain. By integrating advanced gaming features and maintaining a decentralized architecture, Apex Chain establishes a robust and secure environment for the next generation of on-chain games. Built on the strong foundations of Arbitrum and Ethereum, Apex Chain is designed to combine high performance with the resilience needed for lasting and impactful decentralized gaming experiences

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/proof-of-play-apex#connect-your-wallet-to-apex)

Connect your wallet to Apex

Chain ID

70700

Currency symbol

ETH

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.apex.proofofplay.com](https://explorer.apex.proofofplay.com/)

# Liquidity and Yield farming | Camelot DEX

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#v3)

V3

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#how-does-v3-manual-mode-function)

How does V3 manual mode function?

V3 Concentrated liquidity allows liquidity providers on Camelot to set custom price ranges for their tokens instead of evenly distributing them across the entire price range. This means that liquidity providers can concentrate their capital on specific price ranges where they believe there will be more trading activity, while still providing liquidity across a broader range of prices rather than the entire price range

In other words, concentrated liquidity allows providing liquidity for specific prices you like, instead of sharing all your liquidity across the whole range. It's like only sharing your favourite toys, instead of sharing all of your toys, with your friends

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#example-of-the-mechanics)

**Example of the mechanics**

For volatile pair, an LP could provide liquidity for a price range of $1.10 - $1.30. This means that liquidity would only be used within that price range, allowing for more targeted liquidity provision In a stable pair, a liquidity provider may opt to allocate their capital only to the range of $0.995-$1.005. This can result in deeper liquidity for traders around the mid-price, and the LP can earn more trading fees using their capital

_If you would like to learn how to use V3, refer to the following_ [_guide_](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated)

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#what-is-the-difference-between-auto-mode-and-manual-mode)

What is the difference between Auto mode and Manual mode?

*   Manual mode is designed for experienced liquidity providers, giving them control over the price ranges of the liquidity they offer
    
*   Auto mode utilizes focused liquidity management strategies, handling the intricate task of adjusting price ranges for users
    

From the user's point of view, the process is quite simple - If the pair of your position is incentivized with market maker rewards, you will receive additional rewards on top of the trading fees that are harvestable in the positions section of the dapp's interface.

For traders and liquidity providers, what improvements does v3 bring?

Through V2, liquidity providers deposit equal amounts of two assets (50:50) in a liquidity pool, which is then used to facilitate trades between those assets. This can lead to idle capital, as the liquidity provider's funds may not always be utilized fully. Additionally, the fixed ratios of the deposited assets can limit trading flexibility and result in higher fees for traders

V3 benefits liquidity providers and traders by allowing for more efficient trading and reducing slippage costs. Traders can now swap tokens at prices closer to market rates, while liquidity providers can earn higher fees for providing liquidity at the specific price points where there is higher demand

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#how-does-v3-enhance-the-protocol)

How does V3 enhance the protocol?

*   Attracting more liquidity providers: The benefits of V3 CL, such as higher APRs, make providing liquidity more attractive for potential LPs
    
*   Increased trading volume: CL leads to tighter spreads and improved capital efficiency. This attracts more traders to the platform, resulting in higher trading volume which simply means more fee revenues for the protocol
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#what-are-the-main-differences-between-v2-and-v3)

What are the main differences between V2 and V3?

The main differences between V2 and V3 are the introduction of concentrated liquidity, directional & dynamic volatility fees, limit orders, rebasing tokens, custom tick spacing and improved capital efficiency in V3 as well as significant UI updates. These new features allow LPs to customise their exposure and potentially earn higher returns from trading fees compared to the previous version.

*   V2 = 50/50 ratio between assets bundled into LP
    
*   V3 = Custom range
    

*   V3 allows liquidity providers to concentrate their liquidity at specific price points, leading to more efficient use of capital and higher capital efficiency
    
*   V3 concentrated liquidity model allows for more precise pricing and lower slippage for traders, especially in volatile markets
    
*   V3 liquidity range orders can help traders execute trades more efficiently, as they can specify the price range they want to trade in ranges and adjust positions as market conditions change
    
*   V3 offers more granular control over liquidity positions, with the ability to create custom tick
    
*   V3 has lower gas costs and is more gas-efficient than V2
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#does-camelot-charge-higher-fees-for-swaps-that-use-concentrated-liquidity-and-if-not-how-can-the-apr)

Does Camelot charge higher fees for swaps that use concentrated liquidity, and if not, how can the APR be higher when using concentrated liquidity?

The swap fees themselves may not necessarily change based on whether the liquidity is concentrated or not, but the benefits of concentrated liquidity come into play for LPs. By focusing your capital in specific price ranges, as an LP you can potentially earn a higher share of fees relative to contributed capital.

Imagine two pools, one with concentrated liquidity 'V3' and another with a full range of liquidity 'V2'. Both pools facilitate the same volume of swaps and collect the same fees. In the CL pool 'V3', since there's less idle capital, the fees are distributed among a smaller amount of provided capital. This means that liquidity providers in the concentrated pool may receive a higher return even though the fees from each swap remain the same.

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#how-should-price-ranges-be-selected)

How should price ranges be selected?

*   Consider how much prices are likely to move during the lifetime of your position
    
*   Be willing to actively manage the position as the market changes
    
*   Take into account the economics of the transactions required to manage the position
    
*   If prices move outside your specified range, your position will be concentrated in one asset and you won't earn trading fees until prices return to the range
    
*   Providing liquidity across the full range is an option, but it will result in a lower rate of return than a narrower range
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#range-presets)

Range presets

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F8ieDQsGux3apiCv7SQNh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3595ece9-e454-4f61-923e-c85aaf856707&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=951be64a&sv=2)

1.  **Full range** - Liquidity is provided across the entire price range of the asset being traded. This can be useful for assets that have a wide trading range or are subject to high volatility
    
2.  **Wide range** - Liquidity is concentrated in a wider price range. This can be useful for assets with moderate volatility, as it provides sufficient liquidity across a range of prices
    
3.  **Common range** - Liquidity is concentrated in both the buy and sell range around the current market price
    
4.  **Narrow range** Liquidity is concentrated in a specific price range, usually close to the current market price. This can be useful for assets that have relatively stable prices, as it reduces the amount of capital required to provide liquidity while still maintaining efficient trading
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#is-my-position-liquidated-if-the-price-exceeds-my-price-range)

Is my position liquidated if the price exceeds my price range?

If the price of a trading pair goes beyond the range that you set for your LP, then your position will only consist of the less valuable asset in that pair

For instance, if your price range for ETH/USDC is 555-1555, and ETH drops to 550, then your balance will only be in ETH. On the other hand, if ETH increases to 1560, then your balance will only be in USDC

When the price remains outside of your specified range, your position will be in an out of range mode, which means that you will not earn any fees until the price returns to your set range

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#how-apr-for-trading-fees-is-calculated)

How APR for trading fees is calculated?

To calculate the APR for trading fees, we collect the total active TVL and fees made approximately every 10 minutes. We then determine the average active TVL for the past 7 days (or since the pool went live if it has been live for less than 7 days) - Using the fees earned during this period, we calculate the APR

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#can-i-create-a-custom-token-pair-in-v3)

Can I create a custom token pair in V3?

Yes, you can create a custom token pair by providing liquidity to a new combination of tokens that do not have an V3 existing pool. To do so, you will need to select the tokens, set a price range, and deposit the required amounts of both tokens. Once the pool is created, others can also provide liquidity to that token pair

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#can-i-withdraw-my-concentrated-liquidity-at-any-time)

Can I withdraw my concentrated liquidity at any time?

Yes, you can withdraw your position at any time

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F3vvvt8L2ooK8trQqrlnl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ecce2be-da0d-4fed-a929-bd205dec2785&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7374e2a6&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#how-are-fees-earned-and-distributed-in-concentrated-liquidity-pools)

How are fees earned and distributed in concentrated liquidity pools?

Fees are earned from swap transactions that occur within the specified price range set by the liquidity providers. These fees are automatically distributed proportionally to the liquidity providers based on the amount of liquidity they have contributed and the time they have been in the pool. For manual mode, pending rewards are harvestable on the V3 position management panel - when it comes to auto mode the LP fees auto-compounding in the LP

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#will-v2-pools-ever-be-discontinued)

Will V2 pools ever be discontinued?

We have no intention of discontinuing V2. Due to the technical complexities associated with concentrated liquidity, some users/protocols may opt for V2 over V3

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#v2-and-exchange)

V2 and Exchange

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming#why-am-i-unable-to-set-the-amount-in-the-top-box-on-the-frontend-exchange-page)

Why am I unable to set the amount in the top box on the frontend exchange page?

This limitation arises due to the stable logic in place, which precludes calculations in the reverse direction

# Providing Liquidity explained | Camelot DEX

On a Camelot, a liquidity pool is a crowdsourced pool of tokens locked in smart contracts and used to facilitate trades between the assets. Automated market maker (AMM) allow digital assets to be traded in an automatic and permissionless manner through liquidity pools, replacing traditional markets of buyers and sellers

Liquidity providers will receive a portion of each transaction fee and additional incentives if they are provided for the LP pair

# 🔥┃Deflationary mechanisms | Camelot DEX

In addition to the hardcap set on GRAIL, we also implemented some deflationary mechanisms in order to reduce the total supply.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/deflationary-mechanisms#buy-back-and-burn)

Buy back & burn

A share of the [protocol earnings](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings)
 is dedicated to buy back & burn GRAIL, in order to apply a continuous buying pressure on it.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/deflationary-mechanisms#xgrail-redeems)

xGRAIL redeems

When [converting xGRAIL to GRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming)
, if the vesting duration isn't the maximum, the xGRAIL:GRAIL ratio will be lower than 1:1, down to a minimum of 1:0.5. All of the GRAIL excess will automatically be burned.

For instance, if a user redeems 1000 xGRAIL with the minimal 15 days vesting duration, he will obtain a 1:0.5 ratio, and receive 500 GRAIL in the end.

That means a total of 1000 - 500 = 500 GRAIL will be burned during the process.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/deflationary-mechanisms#xgrail-deallocations)

xGRAIL deallocations

When deallocating xGRAIL from a Plugin, a deallocation tax is applied. It can vary between contracts, but will usually be of 0.5%.

The corresponding GRAIL amount will automatically be burned.

[Previous🏦┃Protocol earnings](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings)
[Next🔵┃Arbitrum](https://docs.camelot.exchange/contracts/arbitrum)

Last updated 1 year ago
