# Swapping Explained | Camelot DEX

The swap feature is used when traders want to exchange tokens within trading pairs.

On Camelot, users are charged a [trading fee](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings)
 when they make a token swap. [Liquidity](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/providing-liquidity-explained)
 is provided to the exchange by liquidity providers, who add their tokens to liquidity pools.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-explained#swap-modes)

Swap modes

*   Aggregator (V3) - This mode utilizes the Paraswap and OpenOcean APIs and combines both the Camelot V3 and V2 AMMs (Native mode uses only V3 and V2 AMMs)
    
*   V3 - This mode exclusively uses the V3 AMM
    
*   V2 - This mode exclusively uses the V2 AMM
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-explained#how-to)

How to

[Swap tokens](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/swap-tokens)

For tokens with a custom transfer **TAX**, get familiar with the following [document](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-tax-tokens)

Before initiating the swap, please make sure you are satisfied with the output parameters, such as price impact, minimum received, and rates

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FWWXV9IBhmH8Kp8jeahd5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39422666-cc9f-4dbe-99a5-f045bd7cbfb3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c268623&sv=2)

[PreviousProviding Liquidity explained](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/providing-liquidity-explained)
[NextSwapping Tax Tokens](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-tax-tokens)

# 🌐┃AMM V4 | Camelot DEX

Camelot integrates the 1.2 version of Algebra Integral, offering a powerful, flexible, and user-friendly experience for traders and liquidity providers.

For any technical development details, please refer to the [Algebra Documentation](https://docs.algebra.finance/algebra-integral-documentation/algebra-integral-technical-reference/changes-v1.2)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4#key-features)

Key Features

Algebra Integral (V4) is an innovative Automated Market Maker (AMM) that introduces a modular architecture to enhance the performance and flexibility of DEXes.

1.  **Concentrated Liquidity**
    
    *   Similarly to our AMMv3, LPs can allocate their liquidity to specific price ranges, improving capital efficiency and reducing slippage for trades within those ranges
        
    
2.  **Gas optimizations**
    
    *   All contracts have been extensively redesigned, leading to both gas savings and enhanced functionality for the protocol
        
    
3.  **New architecture**
    
    *   Liquidity storage has been separated from peripheral functionality modules (fees, oracles, etc...), keeping the critical functionality immutable while allowing non-core ones to be updated without any migration
        
    
4.  **Plugin Integration**
    
    *   Plugins enable developers to deploy custom (non-core) logic into pools. These hooks allow for advanced features such as dynamic fees, specialized incentives, experimental trading mechanisms, and many other things, providing unmatched flexibility and innovation potential
        
    
5.  **Support for rebase tokens**
    
    *   Unlike traditional concentrated liquidity AMMs, where tokens from rebase mechanisms remain stuck in the pool, Algebra Integral directly distributes these accrued tokens to liquidity providers
        
    
6.  **Custom pool creation**
    
    *   A key innovation in Integral is the introduction of multi-pool functionality for each token pair. This allows plugin developers to create unlimited pools, each enhanced with unique plugins, enabling unparalleled customization and flexibility
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4#plugins)

Plugins

Think of plugins as "add-ons" or "extensions" for a liquidity pool, similar to how apps enhance the functionality of a smartphone. They allow developers and protocols to introduce advanced features into a pool without overhauling the critical parts of the AMM.

The current beta stage of the AMMv4 will be used to test different plugin setups and configurations in order to optimize their settings.

The current set of plugins used by Camelot is the following:

**1\. Adaptive fees**

*   Allows to adjust the fees of a pool based on its volatility during the last 24h. More info about the calculations on [https://docs.algebra.finance/algebra-integral-documentation/algebra-integral-technical-reference/plugins/adaptive-fee](https://docs.algebra.finance/algebra-integral-documentation/algebra-integral-technical-reference/plugins/adaptive-fee)
    

**2\. Sliding fee**

*   Adjusts the fees on every swap based on the price change of the last block and the swap direction. It increases its value when the trade matches with the direction of the price change, and decreases it for the opposite direction. More info about the calculations on [https://docs.algebra.finance/algebra-integral-documentation/algebra-integral-technical-reference/plugins/sliding-fee](https://docs.algebra.finance/algebra-integral-documentation/algebra-integral-technical-reference/plugins/sliding-fee)
    

**3\. Volatility and TWAP Oracle**

*   Stores timepoints and calculates statistical averages
    

**4\. Security**

*   Enables the option to halt a specific pool—or all pools—during emergencies
    

Many other plugins will be conceptualized and created over time, with some already in development:

**1\. Limit Orders**

*   Allows traders to set specific price points at which they want to execute a trade, similar to centralized exchanges
    

**2\. TWAP Oracles**

*   Provides Time-Weighted Average Price (TWAP) data directly from the pool, a critical feature for price feeds and smart contract integrations
    

**3\. JIT (Just-In-Time) Liquidity**

*   Enables liquidity providers to strategically add liquidity at the moment it's most needed, increasing efficiency and minimizing idle capital
    

**4\. Perpetual and Leverage Trading**

*   Expands the DEX’s capabilities to include advanced trading options, such as perpetual contracts and leverage
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4#custom-pools)

Custom Pools

Integral introduces the ability to create an unlimited number of pools for the same token pair. These pools are categorized into two types:

1.  **Default (or "official") pools**: the standard pools provided by the protocol, that you will see by default and interact with on the frontend
    
2.  **Custom pools**: user- or protocol-deployed pools designed for tailored use cases
    

Custom pools provide a unique level of flexibility, allowing deployers to customize their behavior according to specific needs. Each custom pool can feature its own fee structure and integrate custom plugins, enabling a wide range of use-case-specific optimizations.

Pool deployers can configure a **plugin fee**, granting them a share of the swap fees generated within their pools. This approach not only fosters innovation but also incentivizes the creation of unique and optimized liquidity solutions.

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4#why-is-it-important)

Why is it important?

*   **Flexibility**: Offers users and protocols a choice of pools tailored to specific needs
    
*   **Innovation**: Builders can test experimental strategies in isolated pools
    
*   **Robust Liquidity**: Diverse pools create a dynamic and resilient trading environment
    

#### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4#some-use-cases)

Some use cases

1.  **High-Fee Stability Pools**: Ideal for risk-averse LPs focusing on steady returns
    
2.  **Low-Fee Arbitrage Pools**: Attracts high-frequency traders and arbitrageurs
    
3.  **Experimental Pools**: Builders can deploy unique plugins for targeted strategies
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4#utilize-v4)

Utilize V4

[V3/V4 Add Liquidity (concentrated)](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated)

[Previous🌐┃AMM V3](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v3)
[Next🎁┃Incentive system](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/incentive-system)

Last updated 3 months ago

# 🌐┃AMM V2 | Camelot DEX

Camelot's V2 AMM is based on UniV2 constant formula, with a custom implementation of a Solidly-type logic for stables.

The Camelot AMM is the core of our ecosystem-oriented approach, designed with the following principles in mind:

*   A high level of flexibility and customization
    
*   An optimized trading efficiency for users
    
*   Providing support to protocols' growth by adapting to their needs
    

This reflection led us to develop our AMM V2, which includes a dual-liquidity model for our pairs and introduces dynamic directional fees as well as a swap referral mechanism for partnering apps.

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTv9Xu75KQ5fOCIpfeGLX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07151c94-3e5b-4c62-b8c2-4f5e57e45726&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e67d670c&sv=2)

[Dual-liquidity type](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dual-liquidity-type)
[Dynamic directional fees](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dynamic-directional-fees)
[Referral](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/referral)

[PreviousDistribute incentives](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/guidelines-for-lp-deployment-and-incentives/distribute-incentives)
[NextDual-liquidity type](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dual-liquidity-type)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Referral | Camelot DEX

The swap referral is aimed directly at partners and projects that want to become a part of our ecosystem.

Every partnered project can add its referral address to each transaction made on Camelot through its dapp, and subsequently receives a part of their users' generated swap fees. This results in a win/win situation in which **all Camelot actors are adequately rewarded**, thereby fostering a **fair and sustainable ecosystem**.

The swap referral can only be used by **whitelisted partners.** It cannot be used by single users or unapproved projects.

To inquire about our services if you are a new or existing project developer, please [contact us directly.](https://docs.camelot.exchange/contact-us/partnership-inquiries)

[PreviousDynamic directional fees](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dynamic-directional-fees)
[Next🌐┃AMM V3](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v3)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Manual mode | Camelot DEX

1.  **Set a range**
    

When setting the range, you may either use four presets or enter the minimum and maximum prices according to your strategy. The smaller the range, the higher the yield, but there is also a greater risk of [impermanent loss](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/understanding-impermanent-loss)
 When deciding on a price range, it's important to think about how much you expect prices to change during the time that you're holding your position. You'll also need to think about how much time and effort you're willing to put into managing your position as market conditions change, as well as the costs involved in making those changes

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FCsa847FXCsr5HK7vnjIp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c0a719c-bc68-4343-ae85-83c71a0e3398&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=522890ba&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FUwmQsCBMOfG9fe9tyU6y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66895e74-9c69-4743-ba35-581a46778e46&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=133532ad&sv=2)

If the price of the assets you're providing liquidity for goes outside of the range you've specified, then your position will become focused on one asset or the other. You won't earn any trading fees until the price returns to within your specified range

Please note that the price you enter will be rounded to the nearest tick. It is not necessary to enter a round number, as this is a characteristic of how ticks function

1.  **Input amounts**
    

Input the amount in one box, and the other box will automatically display the corresponding amount. The ratio between the two amounts depends on your price range relative to the market price. If your price range is closer to one side of the market price, you will provide more of that asset. If you click the **Full range** button, you can provide liquidity across the full range, as in V2

Liquidity providers have the option to allocate liquidity on one side of the market, either above or below the current spot price, depending on whether they are provisioning the token with a higher or lower value

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FyfTGr2AY15HoNaOH4S37%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a6bd03e-debc-49b5-8ffd-d911f2651f3d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c50c6ac3&sv=2)

1.  **Approve and Add liquidity**
    

To proceed with adding liquidity, start by granting approval. _(This is solely necessary for the initial liquidity provision involving a token)_

Following approval in your wallet, proceed to click on **Add liquidity,** review the provided details, and then click **Add liquidity** once more to execute the transaction from your wallet

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fzc9IbRszRykm1Q9xMOcM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f0dabe4-0443-4a4b-98c4-4b62bff0093a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=794aa9e4&sv=2)

1.  **Earn and manage**
    

Your assets are now actively contributing liquidity and accruing trading fees and market maker rewards (depending on whether LP pair is incentivized)

You can oversee and monitor your positions by clicking on **View existing positions** after successfully providing liquidity or navigating to the **Earn** tab, then selecting **Positions** and choosing **LP V3**

1.  **Unbind/add liquidity and harvest**
    

On the V3 position management panel, you can view your position data, pending earned fees and incentives. You can also access the following features:

*   Market maker rewards: harvest your pending incentives on the positions page
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F5uKrjANtho0ayplG7b2t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da5e5c66f-0ad8-4512-a9cc-045ef9ed9363&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1536a7e4&sv=2)

*   Unbind: withdraw liquidity
    
*   Add: add more liquidity to your position
    
*   Harvest: harvest your pending rewards
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FhnnQIgzcsSNyFZjchLqF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a83ef4c-06c8-49fc-bb13-924de505163e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46564a4&sv=2)

When you claim your Market Maker incentives, all your pending rewards from every Camelot pool will be automatically collected for you

Note that your pending market maker rewards may appear on the positions page up to 4 hours after your deposit and it may even take longer depending on the size of your position

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated/manual-mode#what-does-the-burn-position-button-signify-when-unwrapping-v3-v4-lp)

What does the Burn Position button signify when unwrapping V3/V4 LP?

The Burn position feature allows you to entirely liquidate your V3/V4 position. Not burning position when closing can be useful if you intend to add liquidity again in the future using the same parameters. If you decide not to burn a position, it will remain empty and available for a future liquidity deposit. If you burn it you will get back the assets that you originally paired and the position will be burned

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F4XNeQ49gvU9RwNkTQkf2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D435d2a3a-fe6f-4a99-be5b-c6ed49c884a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5ccfd851&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated/manual-mode#scenario-example-eth-usdc-pool-or-range-2000-2500)

Scenario example: ETH/USDC pool | range 2000-2500

1.  You've added 1 $ETH and 2250 $USDC to the pool. The current price of $ETH is $2250. Your liquidity is active and earning fees
    
2.  Over the next few days, the price of $ETH increases to $2400, remaining within your specified range. Your liquidity continues to be active, and you keep earning fees
    
3.  The price of $ETH further rises to $2600, now outside your range. Your liquidity becomes inactive, and you stop earning fees. The ETH/USDC ratio in your position has changed due to trades happening within the range; you now have more $USDC and less $ETH in your position
    
4.  After a week, the price of $ETH falls back to 2300 USDC, which is within your range again. Your liquidity becomes active
    
5.  and you resume earning fees
    
6.  After a month, you decide to remove your liquidity from the pool. You withdraw your position, which now consists of 0.91 ETH and 2555 USDC due to trades and fees collected during the time your liquidity was active. The composition of your assets has changed, but the overall value has increased due to the fees earned
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated/manual-mode#single-sided-liquidity-provision)

Single-sided liquidity provision

Single-sided liquidity feature in V3 allows liquidity providers to deposit a single asset instead of both assets in a trading pair. This feature is intended to give liquidity providers more flexibility and reduce the risk associated with providing liquidity.

**Here's an example to help illustrate single-sided liquidity provision:**

1.  Let's assume that Galahad have 0.01 ETH and wants to provide single-sided liquidity on V3 within the price range of 2169-2416 USD for each ETH
    
2.  Currently, the price of ETH is $1856.3, which is outside of your chosen price range ($2169-$2416). This means that Galahad's provided liquidity will not be active at the current price and will not start earning fees until the price of ETH enters your specified range
    
3.  If the price of ETH were to increase and enter the $2169-2416 range, Galahad's 0.01 ETH would then be used as single-sided liquidity in the pool. Galahad would start earning fees from the trading activity involving ETH within this price range. If the price of ETH were to fall or rise beyond your specified range, Galahad's liquidity would once again become inactive and stop earning fees
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FX58zweyoFSDeONn8MrcU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50c86a47-87f9-4a20-b861-1ed97fd66684&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6fc203f3&sv=2)

**Key points to keep in mind about single-sided liquidity provision in V3/V4:**

*   Single-sided liquidity providing allows liquidity providers to deposit only one asset instead of both assets in a trading pair
    
*   V3/V4 uses the current price of the assets to calculate the correct amount of the other asset needed to create the trading pair
    
*   Single-sided liquidity providing can reduce the risk associated with providing liquidity since liquidity providers don't have to worry about the value of both assets in the trading pair
    
*   Liquidity providers can still earn trading fees even if they only provide one asset to the pool
    

Single-sided liquidity providing is useful for liquidity providers who may not have both assets on hand or want to reduce their risk exposure

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated/manual-mode#faqs)

[FAQ's](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/faqs/liquidity-and-yield-farming)

# 🌐┃AMM V3 | Camelot DEX

Camelot's V3 AMM is based on Algebra's V1.9, a cutting-edge tick-based concentrated liquidity solution. For more comprehensive details, you can refer to their [technical documentation](https://docs.algebra.finance/algebra-integral-documentation/algebra-integral-technical-reference/changes-v1)
 and [whitepaper](https://algebra.finance/static/Algerbra%20Tech%20Paper-15411d15f8653a81d5f7f574bfe655ad.pdf)

The AMM operates similarly to Univ3, with a range of custom features that enhance efficiency and performance. Among its general performance improvements on the vanilla Univ3 codebase, some major enhancements have been implemented, such as:

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v3#customizable-tickspacing)

Customizable Tickspacing

V3 AMM empowers users with the ability to customize tick spacing settings for each liquidity pool. This feature unlocks unparalleled flexibility by allowing tailored tick parameters. By providing the flexibility to adjust tick spacing, V3 AMM ensures optimal efficiency for each liquidity pool. This enhanced efficiency translates to improved volume and fee generation

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v3#directional-and-dynamic-volatility-fees)

Directional & Dynamic Volatility Fees

V3 introduces a fee structure that adapts to the underlying market volatility, resulting in significant efficiency gains. The protocol dynamically adjusts the fees for each liquidity pool based on the prevailing volatility, enhancing fee generation and trade volume

One of the notable aspects of this feature is the ability to set distinct volatility-based fee ranges for both buy and sell directions. As a result, each liquidity pool can offer highly tailored fee structures that cater to specific market conditions

During periods of low trading volume, the fees automatically adjust downwards, ensuring that users are not overburdened with high fees in quieter market conditions. Conversely, when the market experiences heightened volatility, the fees proportionally increase to account for the increased risk

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v3#utilize-v3)

Utilize V3

[V3/V4 Add Liquidity (concentrated)](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated)

[PreviousReferral](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/referral)
[Next🌐┃AMM V4](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v4)

# Adding tokens to the wallet interface | Camelot DEX

In order for tokens to appear in the wallet interface, they need to be manually added. Tokens that have not been imported will still be received by your wallet, but they won't show up natively.

1.  The project's official website will provide you with the contract address. Additionally, you can find popular token contract addresses such as USDC, USDT, wBTC and etc. on [https://arbiscan.io/](https://arbiscan.io/)
    

_(Fraudsters create fake contracts that you should always be aware of, always verify the address and source of the contract)_

*   Once you obtain the token address tap on Import tokens
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FwU5sfjryQ7JU3TKkTJar%252Ftoken%2520import%25202.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9746bc9-d785-482c-a20a-74e5253eccde&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bec0461b&sv=2)

2\. Once you paste in the contract address of the token, MetaMask should fill out the remaining details for you. Manually add them if they aren't already there.

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FwghbgzgQzyesosKud19D%252Ftoken%2520import%25203.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3639db9a-d8a6-4637-b2b7-03f4a5fa23bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f71dcef5&sv=2)

When you are finished, tap Add Custom Token

3\. The balance of the token you just added will now appear in your wallet

# Create a direct swap link (Arbitrum) | Camelot DEX

Use the following template to generate a link that allows users to directly import the token address into the swap list menu:

[https://app.camelot.exchange/?token2=PASTEYOURTOKENADDRESSHERE&swap=v2](https://app.camelot.exchange/?token2=PASTEYOURTOKENADDRESSHERE&swap=v2)

Where you see "PASTEYOURTOKENADDRESSHERE," simply replace it with the contract address of your token. Depending on whether you added liquidity to V2 or V3 AMM, adjust the end of the link to either 'v2' or 'v3'

# Community plugins | Camelot DEX

The xGRAIL allocation mechanism is made so that any protocol and/or user are able to provide their very own plugin implementation.

All additional xGRAIL allocations will have to be handled through the xGRAIL token contract itself, and more generally, community plugins will have to comply with some technical requirements to make them fit with Camelot's technical stack.

*   Camelot can't be held responsible for any authorization given by users to a third-party Plugin.
    
*   A malicious or badly made plugin contract could make your xGRAIL stuck forever, so remember to be extra careful before approving a contract asking for an xGRAIL allocation.

# Dual-liquidity type | Camelot DEX

Each Camelot LP can have its own type, depending on the expected price correlation level between the two tokens of the pair.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dual-liquidity-type#volatile-pairs)

Volatile pairs

Volatile pairs are composed of uncorrelated assets, based on the usual UniV2 model, using the standard constant product formula:

x∗y\=kx \* y = kx∗y\=k

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dual-liquidity-type#stable-pairs)

Stable pairs

Stable pairs are used for correlated assets, and will try to maintain a 1:1 transfer ratio as much as possible. The formula is based on the well-known Solidly curve:

x3y+y3x\=kx^3y + y^3x = kx3y+y3x\=k

[Previous🌐┃AMM V2](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2)
[NextDynamic directional fees](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dynamic-directional-fees)

# Swapping Tax Tokens | Camelot DEX

Tax tokens automatically charge a fee when you buy, sell, or sometimes even when you add liquidity or transfer them to another wallet. The tax collected from these tokens is often used for specific purposes, often outlined by the team behind the token

When considering a token to determine if it includes a transaction tax, it’s best to clarify with the team behind the token or look closely at the user interface during a trade

If you see an error message like **"Error: Estimated XXX amount invalid. Check your slippage configuration"** it suggests that the token has a transaction tax. However, this alone may not necessarily mean the token has a tax - the message could appear for other reasons, such as high price volatility

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FPyyz5MxZl4dvp6l6CHot%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D387bc3ca-8ac4-462b-a801-0017edc1b0a0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fea6fe&sv=2)

For most Tax tokens, you’ll likely need to use V2 swap mode, but in some cases, depending on which AMM the liquidity was added, you may need to use V3 mode. To check which AMM the liquidity is added on, look through the [analytics dashboard](https://info.camelot.exchange/home/v2)
 and locate the liquidity pair associated with the token you want to swap on either V2 or V3

**Do not use aggregator swap mode if dealing with a Tax token**. While you can use it in some cases, you might get charged tax multiple times when performing a swap

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJTh5k9396QNbItRNJRj9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5afb3874-5bc7-490b-a287-7f3d73cca7bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47e40ad8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-tax-tokens#how-to-process-a-swap-with-a-tax-token)

How to process a swap with a tax token?

Before initiating a swap, you'll have to increase the slippage, as the tax imposed by the token needs to be factored into the slippage settings.

For example, if the token has a 7% tax, set your slippage tolerance to 7.5% (0.5% default)

To adjust the slippage, look for the ‘gear’ icon on the swap page. Once you click on it, you’ll see a modal where you can adjust the slippage. Once you set the slippage settings, [perform a swap](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/swap-tokens)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTjOwiA9IFJy1qDWxIeTz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48970f7d-d671-49c5-ad0d-6d1ad0d40915&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=febb2434&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F9v4r70dgCE3dUqOgsCWb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43a20d34-589f-4f66-95a9-7a0f9af6dc7c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c0b3ed17&sv=2)

[PreviousSwapping Explained](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/swapping-explained)

# Get xGRAIL | Camelot DEX

To begin utilizing xGRAIL privileges, navigate to the xGRAIL tab within the app and locate the Get xGRAIL section of the user interface (It's also possible to earn xGRAIL through incentives offered by Camelot [farms](https://app.camelot.exchange/pools)
)

As an example, the user converts 100 GRAIL; in return, a user gets 100 xGRAIL

If you plan to convert GRAIL into xGRAIL, it is crucial to understand that xGRAIL requires going through a [vesting period](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/redeem-xgrail)
 before you can redeem it for GRAIL

# Conversion - Redeeming | Camelot DEX

GRAIL and xGRAIL are mutually convertible into each other, but the process is different depending on the direction.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming#grail-greater-than-xgrail-conversion)

GRAIL > xGRAIL conversion

GRAIL can be freely converted into xGRAIL at any time. The process is instant, and the ratio is 1:1.

[Get xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/get-xgrail)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming#xgrail-greater-than-grail-redeem)

xGRAIL > GRAIL redeem

The redemption process to convert xGRAIL to GRAIL implies vesting, the duration of which is selected by the user. The conversion ratio will increase proportionally with the vesting duration:

*   The minimum vesting duration of 15 days will provide a 1:0.5 ratio
    
*   The maximum vesting duration of 6 months will provide a 1:1 ratio
    

If the selected vesting duration is lower than the maximum (ratio < 1:1), the unclaimed excess GRAIL is burned

[Redeem xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/redeem-xgrail)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming#real-yield-staking-plugin-allocation)

Real Yield Staking plugin allocation

While being redeemed, the xGRAIL is automatically allocated to the [yield staking plugin](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking)
, but **only for 50% of its value**.

For instance, if a user was to redeem 1000 xGRAIL, he would earn staking rewards as if he actually allocated 500 of them to the real yield staking plugin.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming#cancel-redeem)

**Cancel redeem**

Any xGRAIL redeeming process can be freely interrupted at any time by the user.

Any cancelled redeem before its end will void the whole process. User will retrieve its entire amount of redeeming xGRAIL, and no GRAIL.

[PreviousHow to use xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/how-to-use-xgrail)
[Next⚖️┃Token distribution](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/token-distribution)

Last updated 1 year ago

# V3/V4 Add Liquidity (concentrated) | Camelot DEX

V3 enables liquidity providers to concentrate their capital within specific price ranges, leading to increased liquidity at preferred prices. Users can choose to employ both manual mode and auto mode, with the latter automating the adjustment of price ranges.

You can access data about token pairs on the [pools](https://app.camelot.exchange/pools/)
 V3 tab or the [analytics page](https://info.camelot.exchange/)

To provide liquidity to V3, navigate to the **Trade** tab, select **Liquidity** and choose **V3**

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTLWmJA5l4dyjCnQM2JnJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae67b1f0-ef3a-4d5b-a6e5-cb84f24d6541&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5e26dba&sv=2)

1.  **Select a pair**
    

Start by selecting the pair you want to use for providing liquidity. Take into account factors like trading volume, TVL, and the potential risk of price volatility in the future.

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FUam77tUK9ReaupX4eXVw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a68709e-b7d5-49ca-8b85-8caaec002f3a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a108a&sv=2)

Also, check if the pair is incentivized with market maker rewards, which serve as an additional layer of rewards

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F383WwlshkhgZoMU4qtDa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9850dc58-4527-4580-b518-27dbbaada04e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a472136&sv=2)

1.  **Select a mode**
    

The mode you choose depends on the specific utility you seek:

*   Manual mode is tailored for experienced liquidity providers, granting them control over the price ranges of the liquidity they provide
    
*   Auto mode employs focused liquidity management strategies, handling the intricate task of adjusting price ranges for users
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fnc1AreEE8MundrQz34sD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd51d396e-5145-4611-8bf5-51891d3bfc34&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=15eeed49&sv=2)

[Auto mode](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated/auto-mode)
[Manual mode](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v3-v4-add-liquidity-concentrated/manual-mode)

[PreviousV2 Add Liquidity](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/step-by-step-guides/v2-add-liquidity)

# Redeem xGRAIL | Camelot DEX

The vesting process allows you to redeem xGRAIL for GRAIL tokens by considering the following ratio and output rates:

*   Minimum duration - 15 days (50% GRAIL output)
    
*   Maximum duration - 6 months (100% GRAIL output)
    

If you choose a vesting duration that's less than the maximum (ratio <100%), the remaining GRAIL will be burned

As your xGRAIL vest, 50% of the amount is automatically staked in the [real yield staking plugin](https://app.camelot.exchange/xgrail/staking)
 earning you rewards while the vesting period continues

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/redeem-xgrail#example-of-the-mechanics)

Example of the mechanics

For example, if you redeem 100 xGRAIL for a 90-day (3-month) vesting period, you will receive 72.3% of the GRAIL output, resulting in 72.3 claimable GRAIL after 90 days. Simultaneously, 50 xGRAIL will be staked in the real yield plugin, generating rewards that you can harvest at any point during the vesting duration

Should a redemption be cancelled before its completion, the entire process will be nullified. The user will then recover the total amount of xGRAIL being redeemed, and receive no GRAIL.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/redeem-xgrail#step-by-step-guide)

Step-By-Step Guide

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FjR57XXFfsbHSptg2LbX2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1be94e99-b05f-4d72-9b3c-d8a046f55c3f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c73a015&sv=2)

[PreviousGet xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/get-xgrail)
[NextEarn Real Yield](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/earn-real-yield)

# How to use xGRAIL | Camelot DEX

xGRAIL is illiquid and non-transferable, but can be used through [plugins' allocations](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins)
, and in the future on approved (whitelisted) contracts providing additional usages.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/how-to-use-xgrail#allocations)

Allocations

Users can freely allocate their available xGRAIL to any plugin to take advantage of its benefits. While xGRAIL is allocated and consequently deposited on the token contract, **it can't be used for anything else**.

Deallocating allocated xGRAIL will withdraw the amount back into the owner's wallet.

A default 0.5% fee will be applied when deallocating xGRAIL

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/how-to-use-xgrail#transfer)

Transfer

xGRAIL is by default non-transferable, except from/to whitelisted addresses. This is made so that essential interactions (like allocations and redemptions with the token contract) and additional usages (for instance with partners specific implementations...) can still be leveraged.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/how-to-use-xgrail#specific-guidelines)

Specific guidelines

[Utilize xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail)
[Conversion - Redeeming](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming)

[Previous🔒┃xGRAIL Token](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token)
[NextConversion - Redeeming](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming)

# WINR | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F9wHX5IxsiCku2MHBHtlT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5079cb11-65f9-473c-aa58-cd21cb993ffe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6a4fe1d&sv=2)

[Website](https://winr.games/)

[Chain Explorer](https://explorer.winr.games/)

[Discord](https://discord.com/invite/winrprotocol)

[Telegram](https://t.me/WINRProtocol/)

[X](https://x.com/WINRProtocol)

The WINR Chain, developed by WINR Labs, is a Layer 3 blockchain purpose-built to address the specific demands of the iGaming industry. Leveraging Arbitrum Orbit technology, this blockchain offers high throughput, low latency, and strong security, making it an ideal foundation for decentralized gaming applications. Tailored for both permissioned and permissionless environments, the WINR Chain fosters innovation while maintaining transparency and trust across the ecosystem. Seamlessly integrated with the WINR Liquidity Pool, the chain ensures smooth and reliable transactions, enhancing the overall gaming experience

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/winr#connect-your-wallet-to-winr)

Connect your wallet to WINR


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout this guide, we will assume that you are using the Metamask wallet since it is the one most people use, the process of setting up a wallet should be very similar regardless of the wallet you choose

1.  The first step is to open Metamask and select the network icon dropdown menu
    
2.  When the pop-up appears, click Add Network
    
3.  The Add a network page will open. Add the following details:
    

Network name

WINR

RPC URL

[https://rpc-winr-mainnet-0.t.conduit.xyz](https://rpc-winr-mainnet-0.t.conduit.xyz/)

Chain ID

777777

Currency symbol

WINR

Block explorer URL

[https://explorer.winr.games](https://explorer.winr.games/)

Once you're finished, click Save

1.  You are now connected to the WINR chain
    

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/orbital-liquidity-network/winr#bridge-to-winr)

Bridge to WINR

Tokens can be transferred to the WINR chain using the Just Bet app

You will need a fraction of ETH to pay for transferring fees from Arbitrum

Gas on the WINR chain is paid in $WINR. Therefore, we recommend transferring it as the first token so you can process transactions

1.  Visit the [Just Bet app](https://www.just.bet/)
     and connect your wallet. You will see the screen below:
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJ4DJJLkusTFIAMBYhLuV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a366d86-c122-420c-ace4-f1ebb7381c07&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d613843&sv=2)

2\. Click Log In and choose your preferred method. (For this tutorial, we will use the Connect Wallet option)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F1jbtX3oMlnfz4So9xw3y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c1293ad-0400-443f-9857-df9af20d573c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bf0009f&sv=2)

1.  Select your wallet provider
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F5aOQb2ZGWN2vvAdbMg4A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f6e1fe6-7159-42d8-95bd-54ab4238934c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72f4da73&sv=2)

4\. Confirm in your wallet interface and accept the WINR Chain settings to add it to your wallet's network list

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJsJvxIQCtDzTA4NpRwuk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f85b8de-4a6f-4bc5-b944-e55cf77f36ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8718cd1&sv=2)

1.  Visit your Just Bet wallet
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FFLIdMawT8Dy58cNRi1Mg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4de4fed5-d71b-43ec-92fb-c0e60d7806ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3125d401&sv=2)

1.  Click Deposit
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FFKXCv07WCEaBWqK0qUpW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc744d1a3-d3e1-462c-8f08-17fe9d754d9e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=30388c8&sv=2)

1.  Select the token and specify the amount you wish to deposit
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FuoHEoif681bSYZdGER6Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D821e3cc0-a933-43c0-8296-6b79ae8b5a88&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4485bff&sv=2)

1.  Click Deposit to Funding Wallet
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FfBICFRDrm7KCWKkPcuAo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D084864a4-7609-4bcf-8bd4-dfe763ae4672&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c0f3ceb&sv=2)

1.  Confirm in your wallet interface
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJsJvxIQCtDzTA4NpRwuk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f85b8de-4a6f-4bc5-b944-e55cf77f36ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8718cd1&sv=2)

1.  Click Withdraw
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTSrlLzSEoZk2IlDDdKhg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ca27b06-22ec-4cae-8bed-e70892e86e04&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1cbdbd9&sv=2)

1.  Select the token and specify the amount you wish to withdraw
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FjrfyneDyQUuBVx5WHWfV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32f1e762-2f0c-4af4-b3d1-e1691aa4c6f9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7551cb61&sv=2)

1.  Confirm in your wallet interface
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJsJvxIQCtDzTA4NpRwuk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f85b8de-4a6f-4bc5-b944-e55cf77f36ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8718cd1&sv=2)

1.  Click Transfer
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FnXLUKwHhUwd3u5jVcfYp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5de9ae5d-07fe-4b66-9da5-9f3ef4cfc0fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=987b60cd&sv=2)

1.  Specify the amount and click Transfer
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FRDyH3DeTP5Vh2qFzwaHL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbca5338-61ee-497d-8450-374ea8bce387&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=223ff80a&sv=2)

1.  Confirm in your wallet interface
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJsJvxIQCtDzTA4NpRwuk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f85b8de-4a6f-4bc5-b944-e55cf77f36ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8718cd1&sv=2)

1.  Wait approximately 10 minutes
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FqKU5BmOtbNNPZfiED03i%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ded5dd3-2d08-4574-b026-38dc5d117bed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fec043d&sv=2)

1.  Click Withdraw
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FXyoif1gqi5jsWTGGqdKy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da39ada1d-fc7f-4eb5-83b7-2d1846d3c8b7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0d1c08f&sv=2)

1.  Select WINR, select the token and specify the amount
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTHuOnFi3HfDedqFMcu1e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa22b671-04c8-4702-b785-ec1c47c5b654&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f74a0dbf&sv=2)

1.  Click Withdraw to your Web3 Wallet
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FrLH2q3hPLPboy5nCpIlP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ee9d478-fb81-49a2-be31-fd6a3fb86ec5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96e4a480&sv=2)

1.  Confirm in your wallet interface
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJsJvxIQCtDzTA4NpRwuk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f85b8de-4a6f-4bc5-b944-e55cf77f36ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8718cd1&sv=2)

1.  Your funds are now available in your wallet on the WINR Chain
    

The transfer should take approximately 10 minutes, but it may take longer during periods of high traffic. Withdrawals to WINR chain should take no more than 1 minute

# 🔒┃xGRAIL Token | Camelot DEX

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FA8P4nEov0CtMrdY9YpaS%252Fxgrail-sm.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De38d41fc-0074-4880-bc52-967747b0021f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f21efe17&sv=2)

Name: **Camelot Escrowed Token** Ticker: **xGRAIL** Chain: **Arbitrum** Contract: [**0x3CAaE25Ee616f2C8E13C74dA0813402eae3F496b**](https://arbiscan.io/address/0x3CAaE25Ee616f2C8E13C74dA0813402eae3F496b)

xGRAIL is a non-transferable escrowed governance token, corresponding to staked GRAIL. It can be earned from farming, or through direct GRAIL conversion.

The central use case for xGRAIL is the ability to allocate it to Plugins. The operation consists of staking xGRAIL into the token contract and assigning the deposited amount to a plugin in exchange for various benefits.

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FtsK8k0vW8rq6V7l1uZyh%252FReal%2520Yield%2520Staking.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbfc2b6e-dac8-4aa8-b13e-6655d0f5de1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=880d0634&sv=2)

[How to use xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/how-to-use-xgrail)
[Conversion - Redeeming](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/conversion-redeeming)

[Previous🪙┃GRAIL Token](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/grail-token)
[NextHow to use xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token/how-to-use-xgrail)

Last updated 1 year ago

# 🏦┃Protocol earnings | Camelot DEX

The protocol transaction fees are distributed as follows:

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings#v2)

V2


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FwbHiIEQADH4V4TdVPH2z%252Fpeev2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3beb3b25-a42e-41f7-be1a-6f6cb2da4d14&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ae136f5&sv=2)

*   60% for Liquidity Providers in LP tokens
    
*   22.5% redistributed to xGRAIL holders through [Real Yield Staking](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking)
     plugin
    
*   12.5% dedicated to GRAIL buyback and burn
    
*   5% to the Operating expenses
    

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings#v3)

V3


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F4IySnryO7jIapkfJihzN%252Fpeev3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D445fa34b-b6c3-4a8a-ac42-b30694fca244&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=220be5a1&sv=2)

*   85% for Liquidity Providers in LP tokens
    
*   7% redistributed to xGRAIL holders through [Real Yield Staking](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking)
     plugin
    
*   3.5% dedicated to GRAIL buyback and burn
    
*   3% to the Operating expenses
    
*   1.5% to Algebra for licensing [V3 AMM](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v3)
    

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings#v3-vaults)

V3 vaults


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F9ICsw0f4ummInudO92v9%252Fgammaaaaa-removebg-preview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05f2721e-aa8b-436a-a171-ce193b1edaa4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6ef4347&sv=2)

Camelot also receives a portion of the fees from Gamma’s vaults, ~⅓ of a 25% performance fees, i.e., 8% of the total, split between:

*   5% redistributed to xGRAIL holders through [Real Yield Staking](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking)
     plugin
    
*   3% to the Operating expenses
    

This ultimately leaves Gamma with 13.25% of gross fees generated by their vaults.

[Previous⚖️┃Token distribution](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/token-distribution)
[Next🔥┃Deflationary mechanisms](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/deflationary-mechanisms)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

AMMv3

AlgebraFactory

0x10aA510d94E094Bd643677bd2964c3EE085Daffc

CodePairHash

0x6c1bebd370ba84753516bc1393c0d0a6c645856da55f5393ac8ab3d6dbc861d3

Quoter

0x60A186019F81bFD04aFc16c9C01804a04E79e68B

# Real Yield Staking | Camelot DEX

The majority of the [protocol earnings](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/protocol-earnings)
 are redistributed to users who allocated xGRAIL to the real yield staking plugin.

Staking distribution can be done in the form of one or more tokens, and happens **continuously** (reward/second), through weekly epochs.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking#epochs)

Epochs

The distribution is based on a weekly epoch logic: every week, a fixed part of the owner-defined accumulated tokens is marked as to be distributed.

The same process is repeated every 7 days.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking#payouts-handling)

Payouts handling

The distribution of those tokens is equally spread over the duration of the epoch, and allocated on a second-basis to every user with a xGRAIL allocation on this real yield staking plugin, proportionally to their share of the total allocation.

In more simpler terms, if we go with the following values:

*   a total of 10,000 xGRAIL allocated to the real yield staking plugin
    
*   a daily distribution of 10,000 USDC
    

If a user has allocated 200 xGRAIL to the plugin, he owns 2% of the allocations and will consequently receive 2% of the daily rewards, ie 200 USDC.

Staking rewards are being distributed continuously, users don't need to wait for the end of the epoch to collect them.

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking#deallocation)

Deallocation

Deallocating xGRAIL from this plugin is subject to a 0.5% fee.

[Earn Real Yield](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail/earn-real-yield)

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking#ui-element-descriptions)

UI element descriptions

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FZ8kV2XiD5BsjPG6G3ef3%252FDividends.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b6c487d-c002-441f-9f25-fef294c3e616&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7bbedf15&sv=2)

[Previous🏆┃xGRAIL plugins](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins)
[NextYield Booster](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/yield-booster)

# Wallet Creation | Camelot DEX

MetaMask is by far the most popular and free wallet software that is compatible with virtually any Ethereum-based blockchain, including Arbitrum the home of Camelot. Metamask will allow you to store any assets, buy, as well as connect to any platform built on top of the Ethereum-based blockchain including Camelot.

On PC, Metamask is available as a browser extension, and on iOS and Android it is available as an app. Browser extension for PC is available for Chrome, Firefox, Brave, Edge, Opera and Edge.

Our step-by-step tutorial below will help you create your own cryptocurrency wallet (We will use Chrome as an example, but the process is the same for all browsers) The process of creating a wallet on iOS and Android is fairly similar the only difference is that you won’t have to install an extension but an App)

1.  Go to [https://metamask.io/](https://metamask.io/)
     and click on the download button.
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F7GkSmISJwKymlDUMuxG6%252FCreate%2520wallet%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3938112-a978-4df3-ae40-3ba353fc3993&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c007cd6&sv=2)

2\. On the next page choose on what device you want to install Metamask

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FQPCLNjc76dU0EkqzSuFN%252FCreate%2520wallet%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a145906-e511-4f1d-8e6b-94889992fc4e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c283b09&sv=2)

3\. Click on Add to Chrome

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FSG9NqJNNyzowAtVqk1rE%252FCreate%2520wallet%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D800b9829-66d0-4989-84aa-6fc1ba76a4a6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=351d3bdd&sv=2)

4. Upon the window pop up click on Add extension

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FYFJP8y2iNuvbojc5h6QP%252FCreate%2520wallet%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deff71ff6-5387-4271-acc3-27c989dc7979&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8df9907&sv=2)

5\. Once the extension installs, click on Get started

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F1IT141mkkjjrhswCwegg%252FCreate%2520wallet%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D841c4b03-11e0-47b4-a1c5-f0ba91ac1a4f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5970a67&sv=2)

6\. Click on Create a wallet

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FUuIpTE8O4SnEIOtzhahx%252FCreate%2520wallet%25206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd25195d5-c843-4ca7-91c6-aa5419e463ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86187e44&sv=2)

7\. Set a password that will allow you to access the Metamask wallet on the device you are setting it up and click on Create

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F2bxdIMCrRJV0VBnFaKkU%252FCreate%2520wallet%25207.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9af4027a-4ffb-4c3e-93f0-d4e4fbdafffd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84979909&sv=2)

8\. Click on Reveal secret words

*   Make sure you store your secret phrase somewhere safe. In the event of a device crash or a browser reset, this is the only way to recover your funds. It is recommended that you write it down. Most people write down their 12-word phrase on a piece of paper and store it in a place where only they can access it. (Make sure you write down the words in the correct order)
    
*   In the event that your seed phrase is lost, MetaMask will not be able to assist you in recovering your wallet, and your funds will be lost forever.
    
*   Never share your seed phrase or private key with anyone, unless you want them to have full control over your funds.
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FPfk3dXJoyS19Ic27qZ9A%252FCreate%2520wallet%25208.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcdc0ac71-eea7-4f81-b01e-4c5e962af1fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2b1467d&sv=2)

After you store your secret phrase somewhere safe, click on Next

9\. Confirm your seed phrase in the correct order and click on Confirm

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FQ3sGo4JL5NoJJqgW4tEP%252FCreate%2520wallet%25209.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea27720-d128-4ea0-a354-883052eac9f7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a42fd4d4&sv=2)

10\. Your Metamask wallet is ready for you to use, click on All done to access it

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FxI7gzqAJ9VMenrQ0X6tz%252FCreate%2520wallet%252010.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3435c13-5fcc-427f-8729-6891616548fd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=257cfaf1&sv=2)

You can view your Metamask wallet at any time by clicking on the extension's icon and placing your cursor on the Metamask icon

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FDDRIndGrBYkP9kF5umiF%252FCreate%2520wallet%252011.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd82c8aef-de99-49c4-8e0c-23aacd5fd163&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab34d56d&sv=2)

Click [here](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/wallet-setup-for-arbitrum-compatibility)
 to find out how to set up the wallet to use it on Arbitrum, the home of Camelot.

[Previous📘┃Arbitrum Guide](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide)
[NextWallet Setup for Arbitrum Compatibility](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/wallet-setup-for-arbitrum-compatibility)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Dynamic directional fees | Camelot DEX

Assuming that one size does not fit all, we provide **adjustable swap fees based on market conditions and protocols' specifics.**

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dynamic-directional-fees#dynamic-and-directional)

Dynamic & directional

Camelot pairs can be configured with their own swap fees, but it's also possible for each of them to be set up with **different values depending on the swap direction** (buying or selling).

As a result, we have the freedom to incentivize every pair differently, depending on the volatility or stability of its assets, as well as on the structure of protocols and their own custom needs (an established project seeking to reduce friction, a newly launched project aiming to stabilize and limit selling pressure, etc...).

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dynamic-directional-fees#fees-handling-delegation)

Fees handling delegation

Each project launching on our AMM and willing to work with us can have its LPs configured with specific swap rates tailored to suit its own strategy.

Ultimately, we intend to provide the possibility for partnering protocols to directly take control of their own pairs' swap fees.

[PreviousDual-liquidity type](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/dual-liquidity-type)
[NextReferral](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/amm-v2/referral)

Last updated 8 months ago

# 🏆┃xGRAIL plugins | Camelot DEX

Plugins are contracts linked to the [xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/tokenomics/xgrail-token)
 contract. Some are native and directly made by the Camelot team (dividends, yield booster, launchpads and more to come...) but others can be freely integrated by anyone from the ecosystem.

Users can take advantage of plugins' unique benefits by allocating xGRAIL to them by directly staking into the xGRAIL contract.

[Utilize xGRAIL](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/castle-tutorials/utilize-xgrail)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FFGPKRfDCtS5n7sdiHJwl%252FDiagramxGRAILrefreshed.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8edad97-cc06-4d2b-9640-cd4532514c0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe66f271&sv=2)

[Real Yield Staking](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking)
[Yield Booster](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/yield-booster)
[Community plugins](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/community-plugins)

[Previous🧑‍🌾┃Liquidity Provision](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/liquidity-provision)
[NextReal Yield Staking](https://docs.camelot.exchange/protocol/xgrail-plugins/real-yield-staking)

# Bridging tokens to Arbitrum | Camelot DEX

Tokens can be bridged to [Arbitrum](https://arbitrum.foundation/)
 using a variety of platforms. This guide explains how to utilize the official bridge and various multi-chain bridges. You could also opt for one of the centralized exchanges that support Arbitrum transfers ⬇️

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fa4ND7xvg8ilF21YxSmxk%252Fdddd.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6c872f4-17d6-4d49-b473-7f1aee44b4f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58626ba&sv=2)

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/bridging-tokens-to-arbitrum#official-arbitrum-bridge-ethereum-to-arbitrum)

Official Arbitrum Bridge (Ethereum to Arbitrum)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Visit Arbitrum Bridge and connect your wallet. Ensure you're on the Ethereum mainnet. You will see the screen below
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FtO3SuTyDnEqYMiWzdvAv%252Fbridge%2520main%25201.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7de2d927-f3c0-4675-8574-e9fcf31bab44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6b5b2ce&sv=2)

2\. Input the amount of ETH you want to transfer to Arbitrum and click Move funds to Arbitrum One

3\. Confirm the transaction in your wallet. Despite being executed on layer 1, Arbitrum's lower gas fees will apply

4\. After verifying the amount, click on Confirm

5\. The transaction will show as pending on the next page

6\. Your ETH is now accessible on Arbitrum, ready to be sent and received

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/bridging-tokens-to-arbitrum#camelots-official-partners-multi-chain-bridges)

Camelot's official partner's multi-chain bridges


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/bridging-tokens-to-arbitrum#relay)

**Relay**

1.  Visit [https://bridge.relaychain.com/](https://bridge.relaychain.com/)
    
2.  Click on Connect Wallet and sign in
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Ft5hteDUvZf26HcuaWueS%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db868910d-964c-4c1c-9a45-93edba649313&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8090bc8d&sv=2)

3.

*   Select the chain from which you want to send funds and the token you intend to bridge
    
*   Afterwards, pick the target chain (e.g., Arbitrum) and the desired asset to receive (e.g., ETH). It's advisable to initiate the process by bridging ETH since it's used to pay transaction fees for swaps on Arbitrum
    
*   Input the amount you'd like to bridge
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTsL5w3BpRpDVXjGlkfgX%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56dbf1af-6cea-4daa-a8ba-65d8a702e10b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7666e81e&sv=2)

4\. Click on Bridge & Swap

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FjRp8GQVdYy8VwR56E47a%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbaf6794-046d-4f60-85f7-0e0f365f8926&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8dde1d4d&sv=2)

5\. Confirm approval in your waller

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F8KRCpTsDJuvA7fdLhiZZ%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc350189b-aa52-468d-9e68-abac61d080c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6b37287&sv=2)

6\. In the following popup, once again Confirm _(you must have enough GAS tokens on the network you are bridging from in order to complete the transaction)_

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FVP6fGK6F8MnILujLFYRL%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a6ee997-1f24-4ecb-ab68-605e6234ed1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a94c7d59&sv=2)

7\. Within a couple of minutes of confirming the transaction, your funds should appear in your wallet on Arbitrum

### 

[](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/bridging-tokens-to-arbitrum#hop-protocol)

**Hop Protocol**

1.  Visit [https://app.hop.exchange/](https://app.hop.exchange/#/send?token=ETH)
    
2.  Click on Connect a Wallet and sign in
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FIrEVOHd8V5tqmaBrSod6%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e1c82e0-4eb5-4886-a3f7-eabfb57d87c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e90156d0&sv=2)

1.  Select the asset that you wish to bridge
    
2.  Select the chain that you wish to transfer funds out of
    
3.  Select the destination chain
    
4.  Input the amount that you would like to transfer
    
5.  Make sure that the amount you will be receiving appears correct
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FfmzTFbQTWHxRBCkIrf7l%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9142e8a2-6b86-4cc7-9da4-63e05ed40824&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd0c3d33&sv=2)

1.  Click on Send and follow the steps in the wallet to process the bridge transaction
    

_(you must have enough GAS tokens on the network you are bridging from in order to complete the transaction)_

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252Fd8kB3DTInWOkbZMHDjAQ%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3cebd67-2750-46e7-a640-ec6a01a883fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d58af8fb&sv=2)

[PreviousWallet Setup for Arbitrum Compatibility](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/wallet-setup-for-arbitrum-compatibility)
[NextAdding tokens to the wallet interface](https://docs.camelot.exchange/get-started/arbitrum-guide/adding-tokens-to-the-wallet-interface)

Last updated 1 year ago

# V3 | Camelot DEX

1.  Go to [https://app.camelot.exchange/](https://app.camelot.exchange/liquidity/)
    
2.  Select the chain you want to deploy on
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FNenBANlHcrQ1T781zLob%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd0b8a67-8817-4e54-ac83-1f9973d183f9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46ae7c95&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to the Liquidity page
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FTLWmJA5l4dyjCnQM2JnJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae67b1f0-ef3a-4d5b-a6e5-cb84f24d6541&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5e26dba&sv=2)

*   Select V3
    
*   Select ''TokenX'' and USDC or another token
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FUam77tUK9ReaupX4eXVw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a68709e-b7d5-49ca-8b85-8caaec002f3a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a108a&sv=2)

*   Select Manual mode
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FjLr7OES5cR4LcG0dBp1n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D67ff8e40-763f-4616-b640-3aeb6b30426d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8a9463a&sv=2)

*   Set a range
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252F7oklqk8d3LGe9up5AiYH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1831ec42-0c00-4a28-a87d-5460138d488a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afb670e3&sv=2)

When seeding liquidity for the first time, we recommend using the full range preset

*   Approve tokens and then add your liquidity (be careful with the rate since you will be the one to define it)
    

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FJYjskLJAXKQbZYiCQzQz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29077406-6e97-48d8-a6aa-2b75a50bc647&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6cf4e5a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.camelot.exchange/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3420642431-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FHBFQDThxW7Uo7iHfOHG5%252Fuploads%252FzRkuwTXTSZEXmb4wcFWG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daeb90698-ee08-45d4-960c-cf993067c1d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8466c216&sv=2)

Note that the price you enter will be rounded to the nearest tick. It is not necessary to enter a round number, as this is a characteristic of how ticks function
